### [105] [Interplay of Anisotropy, Dzyaloshinskii Moriya Interaction and Symmetry breaking Fields in a 2D XY Ferromagnet](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.04104)
*Rajdip Banerjee,Satyaki Kar*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究通过蒙特卡洛模拟，详细分析了二维铁磁XY模型在引入各向异性交换耦合和Dzyaloshinskii-Moriya相互作用（DMI）后对Kosterlitz-Thoulass（KT）相变的影响，并探讨了对称破缺场的作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 二维铁磁XY模型在低温下由束缚涡旋-反涡旋对主导的准长程有序相是凝聚态物理中长期关注且深入研究的问题。本研究旨在探索该模型在引入各向异性交换耦合和Dzyaloshinskii-Moriya相互作用（DMI）等扩展项后，对Kosterlitz-Thoulass（KT）相变的影响机制。

Method: 采用详细的蒙特卡洛（Monte Carlo）模拟方法，研究包含各向异性交换耦合和Dzyaloshinskii-Moriya相互作用（DMI）的扩展XY模型。通过调节各向异性至伊辛（Ising）极限，计算不同温度和DMI强度下的能量、比热、磁化强度、螺旋度模量以及涡旋密度。同时计算了关联长度的二阶矩以探究自旋的空间关联性。

Result: 研究发现，无DMI时交换项促进共线（铁磁）有序，而DMI项诱导自旋倾斜。在存在/不存在对称破缺场的情况下，DMI显著影响KT相变。特别地，U(1)对称破缺的4重和8重对称场h4和h8的效应被揭示，展示了双峰比热曲线在DMI存在下的变化模式。

Conclusion: 该研究为拓扑XY铁磁体的低温相提供了重要更新，当考虑额外的DMI、各向异性交换耦合和/或场项时，为合理设计拓扑自旋系统提供了实用的蓝图。研究结果丰富了在复杂相互作用下拓扑相变的理解。

Abstract: A two dimensional ferromagnetic XY model with its bound vortex-antivortex dominated quasi long range ordered phase at low temperatures is a long standing as well as well studied problem of interest in the field of condensed matter. We conduct a detailed Monte Carlo study of such model with rather unexplored extensions where additional anisotropic exchange coupling and Dzyaloshinskii-Moriya interactions (DMI) together affect the Kosterlitz-Thoulass (KT) transition in presence/absence of symmetry breaking fields. Without DMI, the exchange term promotes collinear (ferromagnetic) order, whereas the DMI term induces spin cantings. By tuning anisotropy upto Ising limit, we document energy, specific-heat, magnetizations as well as helicity modulus and vortex densities for different tempeatures and DMI strength. We also compute the 2nd moment of correlation lengths in order to probe the spatial correlation of the spins. Furthermore, the effect of U(1) symmetry breaking 4-fold and 8-fold symmetric h4 and h8 fields are explored which shows how the double-peaked specific heat profiles changes in presence of DMI. Overall, our findings append many important updates in the low temperature phases of a topological XY ferromagnet when additional DMI and isotropy-breaking exchange and/or field terms are considered and thus providing a practical blueprint for suitably engineering topological spin systems.

</details>


### [106] [The optical Su-Schrieffer-Heeger model on a triangular lattice](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.04123)
*Max Casebolt,Sohan Malkaruge Costa,Benjamin Cohen-Stead,Richard Scalettar,Steven Johnston*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 使用行列式量子蒙特卡洛（determinant quantum Monte Carlo）研究三角晶格光学SSH模型，发现不同掺杂浓度下存在金属-绝缘体相变、键序波（BOW）相和s波超导相，但未观察到增强的磁关联。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究三角晶格光学Su-Schrieffer-Heeger（SSH）模型在不同载流子浓度、电子-声子耦合强度和声子能量下的相行为，特别关注与方晶格SSH模型报道结果的差异。

Method: 采用行列式量子蒙特卡洛（determinant quantum Monte Carlo）方法，通过调节模型的载流子浓度、电子-声子耦合强度和声子能量Ω，分析系统的相变行为。

Result: 在四分之一填充（⟨n⟩=0.5）时观察到金属到绝缘体键序波（BOW）相变，破坏局部C6旋转对称性；在四分之三填充（⟨n⟩=1.5）时，小Ω下发现向另一个BOW相的转变，大Ω下出现s波超导相。配对倾向与有效格点间跃迁符号变化相关，且未发现增强的磁关联。

Conclusion: 三角晶格光学SSH模型在不同掺杂浓度下展现出丰富的相行为，包括键序波相和超导相，这与方晶格SSH模型报道的增强磁关联现象形成对比，表明晶格几何结构对相行为有重要影响。

Abstract: We study the triangular lattice optical Su-Schrieffer-Heeger (SSH) model using determinant quantum Monte Carlo. By varying the model's carrier concentration, electron-phonon coupling strength, and phonon energy $Ω$, we identify two doping regimes of interest. At one-quarter filling ($\langle n\rangle = 0.5$), corresponding to the case of a circular noninteracting Fermi surface, we find evidence for a metal to insulating bond-order-wave (BOW) phase transition that breaks a local $C_6$ rotational symmetry. Conversely, at three-quarters filling ($\langle n\rangle = 1.5$), corresponding to a hexagonal Fermi surface, we find evidence for transitions to another BOW phase for small $Ω$ and an $s$-wave superconducting phase for sufficiently large $Ω$. This tendency toward pairing appears to be associated with the possibility of a sign change in the effective intersite hopping, which can occur for sufficiently large lattice displacements. We also find no evidence for enhanced magnetic correlations in the model, contrary to what has been reported for square lattice SSH models.

### [107] [BosonFlow: A C++ codebase for dynamic fRG and single-boson exchange in correlated fermion systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.04232)

Abstract: We present a unified C++ implementation of the functional renormalization group and the parquet equations within the single-boson exchange formalism for several paradigmatic tight-binding and impurity models at equilibrium. The implementation computes the full dynamic vertex and self-energies, with momentum dependence treated using a truncated unity framework. We implement multiple self-energy flow equations, cutoff schemes, and extensions ranging from the dynamical functional renormalization group to multiloop flow equations that incorporate cutoffs in both the propagator and the interaction. The codebase serves as a reference for recent developments in the fRG and parquet methods for correlated electron systems and provides a flexible foundation for developing new many-body approaches and extensions.

### [108] [Topological Phase Transitions and Their Thermodynamic Fate in Arbitrary-$S$ Pyrochlore Spin Ice](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.04346)
*Sena Watanabe,Yukitoshi Motome,Haruki Watanabe*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究建立了经典烧绿石磁体的统一理论框架，揭示了自旋量子数S与各向异性竞争如何决定拓扑相和临界现象。研究发现整数自旋与半整数自旋在低振幅区呈现不同行为，高振幅区则涉及通量量子化和拓扑缺陷结构，最终通过蒙特卡洛模拟验证了理论预测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在建立经典烧绿石磁体（classical pyrochlore magnets）的统一理论框架，以理解任意自旋S在竞争交换和各向异性作用下的拓扑相分类和临界现象。这为解决自旋量子数对系统相行为的影响提供了系统性方法。

Method: 采用自洽理论框架，通过精确对偶性（exact dualities）分析小w区行为，将缺陷结构映射到拓扑环气体（topological loop gases）。使用配分函数（partition function）的精确分解方法，并辅以经典蒙特卡洛模拟（Classical Monte Carlo simulations）验证理论预测。

Result: 在小w区，整数自旋呈现连续3D XY退禁闭转变（3D XY deconfinement transition），而半整数自旋保持U(1)库仑液体态（U(1) Coulomb liquid）。在大w区，宏观通量量子化为2S的倍数，且物理冰规则（physical ice rule）与涌现Z_{2S}通量守恒的兼容性仅当S≤3/2时成立。S=3/2系统映射到3态Potts模型（3-state Potts model），其一阶转变在有限温度下持续存在。

Conclusion: 研究建立了烧绿石磁体的完整分类理论，揭示了自旋量子数对拓扑相和临界现象的决定性作用。理论预测得到蒙特卡洛模拟验证，为理解经典自旋系统的相行为提供了统一框架，并指出热单极子（thermal monopoles）对连续转变的破坏作用。

Abstract: We develop a self-contained theoretical framework that classifies the topological phases and critical phenomena of classical pyrochlore magnets with arbitrary spin $S$, subject to competing exchange and single-ion anisotropies. In the small-$w$ regime, where the single-ion term favors low spin amplitudes, exact dualities reveal a dichotomy: integer spins exhibit a continuous 3D $XY$ deconfinement transition, whereas half-integer spins remain in a $U(1)$ Coulomb liquid without any transition. In the large-$w$ regime, where the local spin amplitudes are maximized ($|S^z| = S$), the macroscopic flux is quantized to multiples of $2S$. By mapping the defect structure to topological loop gases, we prove that the compatibility between the physical ice rule and the emergent $\mathbb{Z}_{2S}$ flux conservation holds if and only if $S \le 3/2$. For $S=3/2$, this maps the system to the 3-state Potts model, whose symmetry-allowed cubic invariant drives a first-order transition. For $S \ge 2$, monopole contamination breaks the discrete clock mapping. Using an exact decomposition of the partition function, we show that the hierarchical string fusion cascade exponentially suppresses the discrete perturbations, which act as a dangerously irrelevant operator at the 3D $XY$ fixed point, protecting 3D $XY$ criticality. Finally, incorporating thermal monopoles, we show that they act as a symmetry-breaking effective magnetic field that severs defect strings. Consequently, the continuous transitions are rounded into crossovers, whereas the first-order $S=3/2$ transition is predicted to survive at finite temperatures, terminating at a critical endpoint. Classical Monte Carlo simulations for $S$ up to $7/2$ corroborate these analytical predictions.

Abstract: Direct experimental access to orbital states in strongly correlated materials remains a major challenge, despite their central role in driving coupled structural and magnetic phase transitions. In systems where electronic correlations, electron-lattice coupling, and relativistic spin-orbit interactions compete on comparable energy scales, even first-principles calculations often yield multiple metastable solutions, hindering the unambiguous identification of the ground state. Here, we demonstrate that the orbital states of the spinel oxide FeV2O4, which possesses active orbital degrees of freedom on both Fe and V ions, are uniquely resolved by combining valence electron density (VED) analysis based on state-of-the-art synchrotron x-ray diffraction with spin-polarized density-functional-theory calculations. Our results reveal that temperature-dependent rearrangements of orbital occupations drive successive structural transitions that accompany collinear and noncoplanar ferrimagnetic orders, establishing a direct correspondence between orbital anisotropy and spin structure. More broadly, this work shows that experimentally determined VED provides a decisive real-space constraint on competing theoretical solutions, offering a powerful and broadly applicable framework for elucidating the microscopic mechanisms of complex phase transitions in strongly correlated electron systems.

### [110] [Harnessing the VO2 Phase Transition for Automatic Gain Control in Transimpedance Amplifiers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.04594)

To overcome this limitation, volatile resistive switching devices have emerged as a promising alternative, offering intrinsic automatic gain control (AGC). Among these, vanadium dioxide (VO2) devices stand out for their reversible insulator-metal transition (IMT), producing abrupt, energy-efficient resistance changes near the transition temperature (67 C). In this work, a switching device was fabricated by sputtering a VO2 thin film and patterning 200 nm electrode gaps atop it. Before integrating this device into the TIA circuit, its switching dynamics were characterized under electrical pulse excitation. Slightly exceeding the temperature-dependent IMT threshold voltage (Vth) yielded fast and reproducible switching. Complementary pump-probe measurements showed that operating well below TC effectively suppresses short-term memory effects linked to the stochastic nature of the first-order transition. Leveraging these insights, a custom VO2-based TIA was developed, demonstrating variable gain and AGC functionality. Furthermore, applying a constant DC current bias during switching induced self-sustained oscillations (2 pJ per spike) with frequencies up to 60 MHz, consistent with the thermal timescale of the VO2 devices. Overall, these results provide a detailed understanding of VO2 switching dynamics and demonstrate their potential for enabling compact, energy-efficient AGC in high-speed TIAs for advanced sensing applications.

### [111] [Strongly Correlated Superconductivity in Twisted Bilayer Graphene: A Gutzwiller Study](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.04631)
*Matthew Shu Liang,Yi-Jie Wang,Geng-Dong Zhou,Zhi-Da Song,Xi Dai*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究通过变分Gutzwiller波函数方法，在魔角扭曲双层石墨烯（MATBG）中探索强关联超导性，揭示了由弱关联BCS型超导到强关联超导的相变，并发现了一种具有节点能隙结构的向列超导态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在理解魔角扭曲双层石墨烯（MATBG）中强关联与非常规配对之间的相互作用。该材料展现出丰富的超导相图，但强关联效应下的超导机制仍需深入探究。

Method: 采用变分Gutzwiller波函数方法，其中Gutzwiller投影算符$\hat{P}_{R}$允许破坏电荷U(1)对称性以容纳超导序。通过Gutzwiller近似评估基态能量，使用包含关联f轨道和非关联c轨道的8带模型，相互作用包括在位库仑排斥$U$、声子介导的反洪德耦合$\hat{H}_{J_A}$和轨道内洪德耦合$\hat{H}_{J_H}$。

Result: 在填充$ν=2.5$时，相图显示圆顶形费米液体（FL）相将小$U$处的弱关联BCS型超导（BCS-SC）与大$U$处的强关联超导（SC-SC）分隔开。向列超导态在相图的大片区域（包括MATBG的实际参数范围）稳定存在，在大$U$下通过相互作用驱动的超导能隙重构获得具有V形态密度的节点能隙结构。在SC-SC区域，$\hat{P}_{R}$的非对角分量强烈抑制f轨道电荷涨落，同时保持有限的配对序和相当大的准粒子权重$Z$。研究还识别出一种有效费米面体积$=ν+2$的新型小费米液体（sFL）态。

Conclusion: 该研究阐明了MATBG中强关联与非常规配对之间的相互作用，并建立了一个适用于其他强关联超导体的通用Gutzwiller框架。在中等和大$U$区域，传统FL和sFL分别作为最低能量正常相，可能成为SC-SC相的母态。

Abstract: We study strongly correlated superconductivity in magic-angle twisted bilayer graphene (MATBG) using variational Gutzwiller wavefunction where the Gutzwiller projector $\hat{P}_{R}$ is allowed to break charge U(1) symmetry to accommodate superconducting (SC) order. The ground state energy is evaluated via the Gutzwiller Approximation applied to an 8-band model consisting of correlated f-orbitals and uncorrelated c-orbitals, with interactions including onsite Coulomb repulsion $U$, phonon-mediated anti-Hund's coupling $\hat{H}_{J_A}$, and intra-orbital Hund's coupling $\hat{H}_{J_H}$. At filling $ν=2.5$, we map out the phase diagram as a function of $U$ and $J_A$, finding a dome-shaped Fermi liquid (FL) phase that separates a weakly correlated BCS-like SC (BCS-SC) at small $U$ from a strongly correlated SC (SC-SC) at large $U$. A nematic SC state, stabilized over a large region of the phase diagram including the realistic parameter regime of MATBG, acquires a nodal gap structure with V-shaped density of states at large $U$ via interaction-driven SC gap reconstruction. In the SC-SC regime, the off-diagonal (charge-U(1)-breaking) components of $\hat{P}_{R}$ strongly suppress $f$-orbital charge fluctuations while maintaining finite pairing order and a sizeable quasiparticle weight $Z$, distinguishing it from a conventional Mott insulator. We further identify a novel small Fermi liquid (sFL) state with effective Fermi surface volume $=ν+2$. Interestingly, in the intermediate- ($U \lesssim 40$ meV) and large-$U$ ($U \gtrsim 40$ meV) regimes, the conventional FL and the sFL are the lowest-energy normal phases, respectively, potentially serve as the parent states of the SC-SC phase. These results illuminate the interplay between strong correlations and unconventional pairing in MATBG, and establish a versatile Gutzwiller framework applicable to other strongly correlated superconductors.

The saturated magnetization exhibits a quadratic dependence with temperature, indicating the presence of long-wavelength spin fluctuations. Analysis of the temperature dependent resistivity reveals a dominant T3/2 contribution over the typical T2 behavior, signaling substantial coupling between conduction electrons and localized spins. The magnetoresistance shows a linear and non-saturating negative field dependency throughout a wide temperature range below TC, which is compatible with the increasing suppression of spin-disorder dispersion related to ferromagnetic spin fluctuations. A thorough analysis of the anomalous Hall effect (AHE) shows that extrinsic skew-scattering contribution, which is associated to Fe-related disorder, dominates the anomalous Hall response. The systematic separation of intrinsic and extrinsic components reveals that, over a wide temperature range, the intrinsic anomalous Hall conductivity scales linearly with the saturation magnetization, despite the substantial extrinsic dominant background. The linear behavior of intrinsic anomalous Hall conductivity with magnetization is in line with a long wavelength spin-fluctuation framework, where thermal spin disorder lowers net magnetization without significantly altering the underlying electronic structure. These findings reveal Fe1/5CrTe2 as a newly investigated van der Waals ferromagnet where spin fluctuations and disorder coexist with a well-defined intrinsic Berry-curvature contribution to the Hall response.

</details>

*Debraj Bose,Saheli Sarkar,Pinaki Majumdar*

TL;DR: 该研究通过空间非均匀Holstein模型结合Langevin动力学，揭示了纳米界面区域的空间不均匀性能够显著增强电子-声子耦合效应，尽管构成材料的体相耦合较弱。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 金属纳米杂化材料（metallic nanohybrids）实验显示，尽管组成材料的体相耦合较弱，但纳米尺度界面处出现了异常强的电子-声子效应。这促使研究者探究空间不均匀性如何影响电子和晶格谱性质。

Method: 采用Holstein模型的实空间（real-space）表述，结合Langevin动力学进行晶格平衡化。该方法能够计算在空间变化耦合存在下的电子和声子谱函数。

Conclusion: 空间不均匀性本身能够强烈重整化电子和晶格谱，为理解金属纳米杂化材料中界面驱动的输运和相互作用效应提供了微观框架。

Abstract: Recent experiments on metallic nanohybrids have revealed unusually strong electron-phonon effects emerging from nanoscale interfaces, despite the weak coupling character of the constituent bulk materials. Motivated by these observations, we investigate the electronic and lattice spectral properties of an inhomogeneous electron phonon system in which strong coupling is confined to interfacial regions embedded in a weakly coupled metallic background.Using a real-space formulation of the Holstein model combined with Langevin dynamics for lattice equilibration, we compute both electronic and phonon spectral functions in the presence of spatially varying coupling. We find that increasing the fraction of interfacial sites leads to a pronounced broadening of electronic spectral features, reflecting enhanced quasiparticle scattering from lattice distortions, but leaves the underlying band dispersion largely intact.Simultaneously, the phonon spectrum exhibits significant softening and damping, originating from strongly distorted interfacial regions.These modifications result in a redistribution of the Eliashberg spectral function toward low frequencies, producing a substantial enhancement of the effective electron-phonon coupling constant.Our results demonstrate that spatial inhomogeneity alone can strongly renormalize both electronic and lattice spectra, and provide a microscopic framework for understanding interface-driven transport and interaction effects in metallic nanohybrids.

*Maxim Sukharev*

Abstract: The ultrafast nonlinear optical response of molecular ensembles is fundamentally altered under strong light-matter coupling. This approach reveals that while collective cavity delocalization drives the macroscopic nonlinear signal toward a severe harmonic cancellation (an effect termed "spectral starvation"), intrinsic many-body molecular interactions robustly resurrect genuine polaritonic double-quantum coherences (DQCs). Crucially, this dictates that J-aggregates ($J < 0$) uniquely isolate the resonant many-body state below the dense two-exciton scattering continuum, protecting the macroscopic coherence from spatial fragmentation. This predictive framework establishes a direct phase diagram to engineer and protect optical nonlinearities across diverse strongly coupled platforms.

However, recent studies have reported notable discrepancies across several hydrogen-bonded and dispersion-dominated systems, raising questions on the accuracy of the approximations underlying each approach. In DMC, the dominant error is expected to stem from the fixed-node approximation, where the nodal surface is typically taken from a single Slater determinant derived from a density functional theory or Hartree-Fock calculation. In this work, we assess the impact of nodal surface optimization on DMC predictions for 12 compounds spanning diverse NCIs, using a recently proposed antisymmetrized geminal power ansatz with natural orbitals. We find improved agreement with CCSD(T) for hydrogen-bonded systems, while having negligible effect for dispersion-dominated systems. These results provide a practical and computationally efficient route to resolving discrepancies in hydrogen-bonded interactions, while offering insight into the remaining differences in dispersion-dominated systems.

### [122] [Genuine pair density wave order on the kagome lattice](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.03531)
*Han-Yang Liu,Da Wang,Ziqiang Wang,Qiang-Hua Wang*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该研究在kagome晶格的双轨道Hubbard模型中发现了真正的配对密度波（PDW）基态，这是一种在无外磁场下具有非零质心动量Cooper配对的超导态。该PDW相在广泛的物理参数范围内作为主要相出现，其形成机制源于多费米口袋上强烈的亚晶格和轨道极化Bloch态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 配对密度波（pair density wave, PDW）是一种在无外磁场下具有非零质心动量Cooper配对的新型超导态。然而，在微观模型中实现作为基态的纯正PDW相极为罕见且具有挑战性，因为真正的PDW态不包含均匀分量，也不受相同波矢下预存的自旋/电荷密度波序调制。

Method: 研究采用最先进的泛函重整化群（functional renormalization group）方法，对kagome晶格上的双轨道Hubbard模型（two-orbital Hubbard model）进行系统分析。该方法能够处理相互竞争的序参量，并在广泛的物理参数范围内识别主导的基态相。

Result: 研究发现了一个真正的初级PDW相，该相在适合实际材料实现的广泛物理参数范围内从竞争序中脱颖而出。PDW序的关键成因是多费米口袋（multiple Fermi pockets）上强烈的亚晶格和轨道极化Bloch态，这些态抑制了零动量Cooper配对，而促进了不同亚晶格间具有非零总动量的配对。布里渊区边界上三个动量${\bf M}_{1,2,3}$处的简并PDW态展现出新颖的交织序，并能线性组合成拓扑非平庸的手性PDW态。

Conclusion: 该模型可在多轨道kagome材料（如CsCr$_3$Sb$_5$）以及冷原子系统中实现，为实验观测纯正的配对密度波相提供了具体的理论框架和材料平台。研究揭示了亚晶格和轨道极化在促进非零动量配对中的关键作用，为探索新型拓扑超导态开辟了新途径。

Abstract: The pair density wave (PDW) is a novel superconducting state with non-zero center-of-mass momentum Cooper pairing in the absence of external magnetic fields. Its realization in microscopic models as the ground state is very rare and extremely challenging, because a genuine PDW state is free of a uniform component or modulations by a pre-existing spin/charge density wave order at the same wavevector. Here, we report the discovery of a genuine primary PDW phase in a two-orbital Hubbard model on the kagome lattice by state-of-art functional renormalization group studies. It emerges out of competing orders over a wide physical parameter range suitable for realistic material realizations. The key ingredients in favor of the PDW order are the strongly sublattice and orbital polarized Bloch states on multiple Fermi pockets. They force the zero-momentum Cooper pairing to involve the same sublattices and be suppressed by onsite Coulomb repulsion, while pairing between different sublattices to be dominated by different Fermi pockets with nonzero total momentum. The degenerate PDW states at three momenta ${\bf M}_{1,2,3}$ on the Brillouin zone boundary exhibit novel intertwined order and can linearly combine into topologically nontrivial chiral PDW states. We propose that the model can be realized in multiorbital kagome materials such as CsCr$_3$Sb$_5$ as well as cold atom systems.

### [123] [Analytical evaluation of surface barrier and resistance in iron-based superconducting multilayers for Superconducting Radio-Frequency applications](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.03702)

Conclusion: 论文最后讨论了提高工作温度（operating temperatures）的前景和未来应用方向，为铁基超导体在加速器技术中的进一步发展提供了展望。

Abstract: New superconducting materials, particularly iron-based superconductors (IBS), have recently attracted attention for their potential applications in particle detectors and accelerators. This paper discusses the application of these materials in multilayer structures for radio-frequency resonators used to accelerate charged particles, with the aim of improving performance compared to bulk niobium. These materials are compared with previously studied multilayers composed of conventional superconductors in terms of the maximum magnetic field they can withstand, their surface resistance, and their power loss per unit surface area. Abstract: We report the design and implementation of a point-contact spectroscopy (PCS) system integrated with a dilution refrigerator, enabling measurements down to 30 mK. The setup employs a needle-anvil geometry with a cryogenic piezo-driven nanopositioner for in-situ formation of mesoscopic point contacts. We discuss the thermal anchoring strategies that enable efficient cooling of the probe to ultra-low temperatures and reliable measurements. The spectra exhibit well-defined superconducting features that systematically diminish with increasing temperature and magnetic field. The platform provides a robust and versatile tool for spectroscopic investigations of superconductors and other quantum materials at millikelvin temperatures and high magnetic fields.

### [125] [Disentangling electronic and phononic contributions to high-temperature superconductivity in X2MH6 hydrides](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.04151)
*Feng Zheng,Shiya Chen,Zhen Zhang,Renhai Wang,Feng Zhang,Zi-zhong Zhu,Cai-Zhuang Wang,Vladimir Antropov,Yang Sun,Kai-Ming Ho*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该研究通过解耦X2MH6氢化物超导家族中的声子与电子贡献，揭示了等电子取代对超导转变温度（Tc）的影响机制，发现电子贡献起主导作用，并建立了基于X-H键距、氢的电子局域函数网络值和费米能级氢投影态密度的综合品质因数，为设计新型高Tc氢化物超导体提供了指导。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解控制超导性的因素对于通过高通量元素取代发现新型超导材料至关重要。研究聚焦于近期预测的常压超导X2MH6家族，旨在解耦声子与电子对Tc的贡献，以确定等电子取代如何改变超导性。

Method: 通过分析X2MH6氢化物家族，解耦声子（phononic）和电子（electronic）对超导转变温度（Tc）的贡献。识别影响电子贡献的三个关键参数：X-H键距（bond distance）、氢的电子局域函数网络值（electron localization function networking value）和费米能级（Fermi level）的氢投影态密度（density of states）。

Result: 等电子取代同时影响声子和电子性质，但电子贡献在决定X2MH6家族的Tc中起主导作用。基于三个关键参数推导出的综合品质因数（figure of merit）在整个家族中与Tc呈现稳健相关性。压力对超导性产生竞争效应：通过缩短X-H键增强电子贡献，但同时通过增加声子频率削弱声子贡献。

Conclusion: Tc的压力依赖性源于电子与声子贡献之间的平衡。通过解耦和分析电子与声子机制，该工作为X2MH6氢化物的超导性提供了全面见解，并为设计新型高Tc氢化物超导体提供了实用指导。

Abstract: Understanding the factors that control superconductivity is essential for discovering new superconducting materials using high-throughput elemental substitution. Focusing on the recently predicted ambient-pressure superconducting X2MH6 family, we disentangle the phononic and electronic contributions to Tc to determine how isoelectronic substitution alters superconductivity. While substitution affects both phononic and electronic properties, the electronic contribution plays the dominant role in determining Tc in the X2MH6 family. We show that the electronic contribution is affected by three key factors: the X-H bond distance, the electron localization function networking value of hydrogen, and the hydrogen-projected density of states at the Fermi level. A combined figure of merit derived from these parameters exhibits a robust correlation with Tc across the family. We further show that pressure produces competing effects on superconductivity: it enhances the electronic contribution by shortening X-H bonds, but simultaneously weaken the phononic contribution by increasing phonon frequencies. The net pressure dependence of Tc therefore results from the balance between these opposing tendencies. By disentangling and analyzing the electronic and phononic mechanisms, this work provides comprehensive insight into superconductivity in X2MH6 hydrides and offers practical guidance for designing new high-Tc hydride superconductors.

### [126] [Multimodal Terahertz Spectroscopy of the Pairing Symmetry and Normal-State Pseudogap in (La,Pr)$_3$Ni$_2$O$_7$ Films](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.04421)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: The discovery of ambient-pressure superconductivity in compressively strained (La,Pr)$_3$Ni$_2$O$_7$ thin films has intensified efforts to identify the pairing mechanism. However, the symmetry of the superconducting order parameter and the character of the normal state remain unsettled. Here we combine bulk-sensitive terahertz (THz) time-domain spectroscopy with THz third-harmonic generation to present spectroscopic insights into these issues. Linear THz spectroscopy reveals a bulk superconducting response in the (La,Pr)$_3$Ni$_2$O$_7$ films, evidenced by the suppression of low-frequency spectral weight below the onset critical temperature, $T_\mathrm{c}^{\mathrm{onset}}$. A weak coherence peak near $T_\mathrm{c}^{\mathrm{onset}}$, together with substantial residual low-frequency conductivity as $T\to 0$, is consistent with disordered $s_{\pm}$-wave pairing. In the nonlinear regime, the third-harmonic signal rises sharply on cooling through $T_\mathrm{c}^{\mathrm{onset}}$, providing an independent signature of the transition. Strikingly, the nonlinear response persists above $T_\mathrm{c}^{\mathrm{onset}}$, pointing to either disorder-enhanced nonlinearity or a distinct correlated normal state. Motivated by angle-resolved photoemission spectroscopy on similarly grown films that identifies a comparable temperature scale, we associate the anomalous normal-state terahertz nonlinearity with a pseudogap. These results establish (La,Pr)$_3$Ni$_2$O$_7$ as a bulk superconductor with $s_{\pm}$-like pairing that coexists with, and may compete with, a distinct ordered state, providing a platform for exploring unconventional superconductivity beyond cuprates and pnictides.

Abstract: Ruddlesden-Popper (RP) nickelates have recently emerged as a new family of high-temperature superconductors. In bilayer RP nickelates, magnetic excitations with large exchange couplings have been observed, supporting a spin-mediated pairing mechanism. Whether comparable spin correlations persist in trilayer nickelates, however, remains unknown. Here, we present a Ni $L$-edge resonant inelastic X-ray scattering (RIXS) study of La$_4$Ni$_3$O$_{10}$ single crystals. While the orbital excitations remain similar to those of La$_3$Ni$_2$O$_{7}$, the collective spin excitations in La$_4$Ni$_3$O$_{10}$ exhibit a comparable bandwidth of about $60$ meV but substantially suppressed spectral weight, implying a weaker electronic correlation in the trilayer compounds. Our results underscore the three-dimensional and multi-orbital electronic character in La$_4$Ni$_3$O$_{10}$, highlighting important differences from the bilayer nickelates. These findings provide crucial insights into the evolution of magnetism across the RP nickelate family and its connection to superconductivity.

### [128] [Discovery of Quasi One Dimensional Superconductivity in PtPb3Bi](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.04653)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: PtPb3Bi在3.01(1) K以下表现出II型超导性（type II superconductivity），具有完全能隙的各向同性s波态和中等电子-声子耦合。该化合物在280(1) K经历电荷密度波相变，电子结构计算显示准一维方向的强色散和横向平面的相对平坦能带，导致显著的费米面嵌套。Wannier电荷中心流和表面态色散证实了非平庸能带拓扑。

Conclusion: PtPb3Bi被确认为一种具有非平庸电子结构的新型准一维超导体，是拓扑超导的潜在候选材料。其同时存在的超导性、电荷密度波和非平庸拓扑特性为研究维度降低体系中的交织量子相提供了重要范例。

Abstract: Quasi one dimensional materials provide a compelling platform where reduced dimensionality stabilizes intertwined topological and superconducting phases. Here we report superconductivity in a new Bi based quasi 1D compound, PtPb3Bi, which hosts a nontrivial electronic structure. It exhibits type II superconductivity below 3.01(1) K. Heat capacity and transverse field muon spin rotation relaxation (muSR) measurements demonstrate a fully gapped isotropic s wave state with moderate electron phonon coupling, while zero field muSR confirms the preservation of time reversal symmetry (TRS). Transport measurements reveal low carrier mobility with diffusive normal state transport. Electronic structure calculations show strong dispersion along the quasi 1D direction and relatively flatter bands in the transverse plane, giving rise to pronounced Fermi surface nesting in the kx-ky plane. Consistent with this, the compound undergoes a charge density wave transition at 280(1) K. The flow of Wannier charge centers, together with surface state dispersion, establishes nontrivial band topology. These results identify PtPb3Bi as a new quasi 1D superconductor with nontrivial electronic structure and a promising candidate for topological superconductivity.

### [129] [Two-Channel Allen-Dynes Framework for Superconducting Critical Temperatures: Blind Predictions Across Five Orders of Magnitude and a Quantum-Metric No-Go Result](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.04719)
*Jian Zhou*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个双通道Allen-Dynes框架扩展，统一了声子介导和自旋涨落介导的超导配对通道，实现了对19种超导材料临界温度（Tc）的准确预测，R²=0.96，跨越五个数量级（0.4-250 K）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有超导临界温度预测框架通常单独处理声子介导或自旋涨落介导的配对机制，缺乏统一描述不同超导材料中多种配对通道的综合方法。需要开发一个能够整合两种主要配对机制的理论框架，以实现对广泛超导材料Tc的准确预测。

Method: 提出了双通道Allen-Dynes框架扩展：通道1采用标准Allen-Dynes公式，包含材料特定的电子-声子耦合（electron-phonon coupling）；通道2引入从非弹性中子散射数据提取的自旋涨落耦合参数（spin-fluctuation coupling parameter）。该框架无需自由参数，对19种材料进行盲预测。

Result: 对涵盖常规超导体、MgB₂、铁基超导体（iron pnictides）、铁硫族化合物（iron chalcogenides）、重费米子（heavy fermions）、铜氧化物（cuprates）和氢化物（hydrides）的19种材料进行盲预测，R²=0.96，Tc范围跨越五个数量级（0.4-250 K）。研究还证明Peotta-Torma几何超流权重（geometric superfluid weight）不能作为Tc的通用预测因子。

Conclusion: 该统一框架成功识别出自旋涨落通道是增强非常规超导体Tc的主要贡献者，为设计Tc超过100 K的材料提供了定量设计规则。框架的预测能力表明整合多种配对机制对于准确描述超导临界温度至关重要。

Abstract: We present a two-channel extension of the Allen-Dynes framework that unifies phonon-mediated and spin-fluctuation-mediated pairing channels for predicting superconducting critical temperatures. Channel 1 employs the standard Allen-Dynes formula with material-specific electron-phonon coupling; Channel 2 incorporates a spin-fluctuation coupling parameter extracted from inelastic neutron scattering data. Blind predictions for 19 materials spanning conventional superconductors, MgB2, iron pnictides, iron chalcogenides, heavy fermions, cuprates, and hydrides achieve R-squared = 0.96 across five orders of magnitude in Tc (0.4-250 K) without free parameters. We further demonstrate a quantum-metric no-go result: the Peotta-Torma geometric superfluid weight, while essential for flat-band systems, cannot serve as a universal predictor of Tc because it correlates with band-structure topology rather than pairing strength. The framework identifies the spin-fluctuation channel as the dominant contributor to Tc enhancement in unconventional superconductors, providing quantitative design rules for materials with Tc above 100 K.

### [130] [Topological surface states revealed by the Zeeman effect in superconducting UTe2](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.04883)
*Zhen Zhu,Hans Christiansen,Yudi Huang,Kaiming Liu,Zheyu Wu,Shanta R. Saha,Johnpierre Paglione,Alexander G. Eaton,Andrej Cabala,Michal Vališka,Rafael M. Fernandes,Andreas Kreisel,Brian M. Andersen,Vidya Madhavan*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本研究通过矢量磁场扫描隧道显微镜（vector magnetic-field scanning tunnelling microscopy）在自旋三重态超导体UTe₂中首次获得拓扑表面态（topological surface states）的直接光谱证据，为寻找本征拓扑超导体提供了关键的光谱指纹。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本征拓扑超导体（intrinsic topological superconductors）具有受保护边界态和非阿贝尔统计特性，但这类量子材料极为稀少。尽管有大量理论预测，但拓扑表面态（TSS）的实验确认一直难以实现，需要明确的光谱证据来验证这些理论预言。

Method: 研究采用矢量磁场扫描隧道显微镜（vector magnetic-field scanning tunnelling microscopy）进行原子尺度光谱测量。通过分析不同原子位点的超导特性，并施加磁场观察光谱响应，结合谱函数计算（spectral-function calculations）纳入塞曼耦合（Zeeman coupling）效应进行理论验证。

Result: 实验发现显著的位点依赖超导性（site-dependent superconductivity）：Te位点存在大的带隙内态密度（in-gap density of states）几乎填满超导能隙，而相邻原子位点保持能隙。磁场作用下，Te位点的带隙内态被选择性抑制，产生空间均匀的超导态。这种位点选择性能隙演化与UTe₂中具有主导Te轨道特征的拓扑表面态理论预测定量一致。

Conclusion: 研究结果为超导体中长期寻找的拓扑表面态提供了明确的光谱指纹（spectroscopic fingerprint），并确立了UTe₂作为探索本征拓扑超导性（intrinsic topological superconductivity）的有力系统。光谱函数计算结合塞曼耦合成功复现了观察到的磁场响应。

Abstract: Intrinsic topological superconductors with protected boundary modes obeying non-Abelian statistics constitute a vanishingly small class of quantum materials. A defining spectroscopic signature of such phases is the presence of in-gap topological surface states (TSS). However, despite extensive theoretical proposals, their unambiguous experimental identification has remained elusive. Here we use vector magnetic-field scanning tunnelling microscopy to obtain direct spectroscopic evidence of TSS in the spin-triplet superconductor UTe2. Atomic-scale spectroscopy reveals striking site-dependent superconductivity: Te sites host a large in-gap density of states that nearly fills the superconducting gap, whereas neighboring atomic sites remain gapped. Upon application of a magnetic field, the in-gap states on the Te sites are selectively suppressed, yielding a spatially homogeneous superconducting state with a markedly deeper gap relative to zero field. This site-selective gap evolution is in quantitative agreement with theoretical predictions for TSS in UTe2 that possess dominant Te-orbital character. Spectral-function calculations incorporating the Zeeman coupling reproduce the observed magnetic-field response. Our results provide a spectroscopic fingerprint of the long-sought TSS in superconductors and establish UTe2 as a compelling system for exploring intrinsic topological superconductivity.

</details>

Abstract: The control of complex laboratory instrumentation often requires significant programming expertise, creating a barrier for researchers lacking computational skills. Through a case study involving the implementation of a setup that can be used as a single-pixel camera or a scanning photocurrent microscope, we demonstrate how ChatGPT can facilitate the creation of custom scripts for instrumentation control, significantly reducing the technical barrier for experimental customization. Building on this capability, we further illustrate how LLM-assisted tools can be extended into autonomous AI agents capable of independently operating laboratory instruments and iteratively refining control strategies. This approach underscores the transformative role of LLM-based tools and AI agents in democratizing laboratory automation and accelerating scientific progress.

### [132] [Electrostatic skeletons and condition of strict descent](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.03861)
*Linhang Huang*

Main category: math.CV

TL;DR: 本文证明了具有对称线的四边形存在唯一静电骨架（electrostatic skeleton），并讨论了静电骨架存在的自然条件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Eremenko猜想每个凸多边形都存在唯一的静电骨架（electrostatic skeleton），该猜想已在三角形和正多边形中得到证明。本文旨在将这一结果推广到更广泛的四边形类别。

Method: 采用共形几何（conformal geometry）的论证方法，特别针对具有对称线（line of symmetry）的四边形进行分析。

Result: 证明了具有对称线的四边形存在唯一的静电骨架，从而部分证实了Eremenko猜想。同时讨论了静电骨架存在的自然条件。

Conclusion: 研究结果为Eremenko猜想提供了新的支持证据，将静电骨架的存在性证明扩展到了具有对称性的四边形类别。

Abstract: Given a precompact domain $Ω\subseteq\mathbb{R}^2$, the electrostatic skeleton of $Ω$ is defined as a positive measure inside $Ω$, supported on a set with no simple loops, which generates $\partial Ω$ as an equipotential curve. Eremenko conjectured that every convex polygon admits a unique electrostatic skeleton. This conjecture has since been proven for triangles and regular polygons. In this paper, we will prove the conjecture for quadrilaterals with a line of symmetry using arguments from conformal geometry. We will also discuss a natural condition that implies the existence of electrostatic skeletons.

### [133] [A Foundation for Gravitational-Wave Population Inference within the LISA Global Fit](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.03390)
*Alexander W. Criswell,Sharan Banagiri,Vera Delfavero,Maria Jose Bustamante-Rosell,Stephen R. Taylor,Robert Rosati*

Main category: astro-ph.IM

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种新的引力波群体推断方法，通过直接评估完整的层次化群体似然函数，解决LISA（激光干涉空间天线）数据分析中同时处理已分辨信号、未分辨随机前景噪声以及共享天体物理群体的挑战。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA数据分析采用基于单事件后验的后处理方法近似评估层次化群体似然函数，但LISA数据分析面临两个主要挑战：需要同时建模所有信号和噪声的"全局拟合"方法，以及已分辨信号与未分辨随机"银河系前景"之间的循环依赖关系。

Method: 本文开发了一种统计形式体系，用于联合推断已分辨引力波源、未分辨随机前景噪声以及共享的底层天体物理群体，并提出了PELARGIR——一个用于LISA全局拟合的GPU加速群体推断原型模块。

Result: 通过玩具模型分析展示了该形式体系和PELARGIR的功能，并规划了实现具有天体物理动机的LISA全局拟合的路线图，该框架可嵌入群体推断功能。

Conclusion: 虽然本文将该形式体系应用于LISA银河系双星群体，但其适用范围涵盖整个引力波谱，包括脉冲星计时和下一代地面观测站等应用场景。

Abstract: Population inference in gravitational-wave astronomy allows us to connect individual detections to the astrophysics of compact objects and their environments. Current approaches employed for population inference with LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA data approximate evaluation of the hierarchical population likelihood via post-processing of individual-event posteriors. However, the case of the Laser Interferometer Space Antenna (LISA) will be more complex for two main reasons: the transdimensional "global fit" approach to LISA data analysis which models all signals and noise simultaneously, and the presence of both individually-resolved signals and the unresolved stochastic ``Galactic foreground" arising from the Galactic binary population, which induces a circular dependence between the resolved and unresolved systems and our ability to detect the former. These challenges are not without opportunity; LISA's data will contain every mHz compact binary in the Milky Way -- either individually or within the Galactic foreground -- with great potential for Galactic and stellar astrophysics. We therefore propose an alternative approach: direct evaluation of the full hierarchical population likelihood within the LISA global fit. We develop a statistical formalism for joint inference of individually-resolved gravitational-wave sources, an unresolved stochastic foreground, and a shared, underlying astrophysical population, present PELARGIR, a prototype GPU-accelerated population inference module for the LISA global fit, demonstrate the formalism and PELARGIR via a toy model analysis, and lay out a roadmap towards an astrophysically-motivated LISA global fit with embedded population inference. While we apply the formalism here to the population of LISA Galactic binaries, it is applicable across the gravitational-wave spectrum with use cases in pulsar timing and next-generation terrestrial observatories.

### [134] [Varieties of electrically charged physical states in SU(2)$\times$U(1) lattice gauge Higgs theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01166)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用淬火（quenched）SU(2)×U(1)规范希格斯理论的晶格模型，耦合一个静态矢量费米子（static vector-like fermion），该费米子与希格斯场处于相同的规范群表示。通过晶格研究分析带电费米子态的传播特性。

Result: 研究发现中性静态费米子比任何带电费米子态都轻得多，这在意料之中。更重要的是，对带电费米子态传播的晶格研究显示，在带电粒子谱中存在至少两个具有不同质量的粒子态。

Conclusion: 该工作成功构造了与先前已知态正交的新型带电/中性粒子态，扩展了电弱理论中物理粒子态的完整图景。带电谱中多个质量态的存在揭示了更丰富的粒子结构。

Abstract: We consider a quenched SU(2)$\times$U(1) gauge Higgs theory on the lattice, coupled to a static vector-like fermion which, in this case, is in the same gauge group representation as the Higgs field. Physical (i.e. locally gauge invariant) electrically charged and electrically neutral states of matter particles in the electroweak theory were described decades ago, but those constructions do not exhaust all the possibilities, and new types of electrically charged/neutral states, orthogonal to former constructions, are described here. The difference has to do with how the static source, which by itself does not create a physical state, is dressed by dynamical fields. We find that, unsurprisingly, the neutral static fermion is much lighter than any of the charged fermion states. But a lattice study of the propagation of the charged fermion states indicates the existence of (at least) two particle states with different masses in charged particle spectrum.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在量子计算机上模拟晶格规范理论（lattice gauge theories）面临独特挑战，需要开发新的理论框架。轨道折叠晶格方法为任意维度SU(N)规范理论的模拟提供了可扩展方案。

Method: 提出了三项具体改进：1）两个新的简化哈密顿量（Hamiltonians）；2）使用更少量子比特的SU(2)理论编码方案；3）通过在哈密顿量中添加额外项，降低达到Kogut-Susskind极限所需的大标量质量要求。

Result: 这些改进显著减少了量子模拟的电路深度和量子比特需求。通过在(2+1)维SU(2)理论上进行蒙特卡洛模拟（Monte Carlo simulations）基准测试，初步结果验证了这些发展的有效性。

Abstract: Simulating lattice gauge theories on quantum computers presents unique challenges that drive the development of novel theoretical frameworks. The orbifold lattice approach offers a scalable method for simulating SU($N$) gauge theories in arbitrary dimensions. In this work, we present three improvements: (i) two new simplified Hamiltonians, (ii) an encoding of the SU(2) theory with smaller number of qubits, and (iii) a reduction in the requirement for large scalar masses to reach the Kogut-Susskind limit, achieved via the inclusion of an additional term in the Hamiltonian. These advancements significantly reduce circuit depth and qubit requirements for quantum simulations. We benchmarked these improvements using Monte Carlo simulations of SU(2) in (2+1) dimensions. Preliminary results demonstrate the effectiveness of these developments and further validate the use of noncompact variables as a promising framework for scalable quantum simulations of gauge theories.

### [136] [Anatomy of a Complex Crystallization Pathway](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.03413)
*Charlotte Shiqi Zhao,Domagoj Fijan,Sharon C. Glotzer*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 通过分子动力学模拟研究两种形成相同复杂晶体结构但粒子相互作用本质不同的系统，发现尽管相互作用起源不同，但两者具有相同的晶体多型体，并遵循相同的多步结晶路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在探究粒子相互作用本质不同的系统是否具有相似的结晶行为，特别是比较各向同性对势（isotropic pair potential）的金属化合物系统与由涌现熵力（emergent entropic forces）驱动的硬多面体系统。

Method: 采用分子动力学模拟（molecular dynamics simulations）方法，研究两个示例性系统：一个由通过各向同性对势相互作用的点粒子组成，另一个由相互作用源于涌现熵力的硬多面体组成。

Result: 两个系统都是多型体（polymorphic）且共享相同的晶体多型体（crystal polymorphs），遵循相同的多步结晶路径（multistep crystallization pathways），在单粒子水平上的局部结构演化也相似。

Abstract: Using molecular dynamics simulations, we investigate the crystallization pathways of two exemplary systems that form the same complex crystal structure but differ fundamentally in the nature of their particle interactions. One system is composed of point particles interacting via an isotropic pair potential characteristic of metallic compounds, while the other system contains hard polyhedra whose interactions arise from emergent entropic forces. Despite the stark difference in the origins of the particle interactions, we find that both systems are polymorphic and share the same crystal polymorphs. Moreover, the two systems follow the same multistep crystallization pathways, and by examining the complex crystallization pathways on the single particle level, we find that the local structure evolution of the two systems is also similar. By mapping the hard particle system's interaction to an effective pairwise potential, we find that such resemblance arises from the particle interactions being effectively similar.

### [137] [Shear Banding in Simulations of Polymer Melts](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.03424)
*Lucas L. Nelson,Gary S. Grest,Peter D. Olmsted*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究通过数值模拟与理论模型对比，探讨了聚合物在剪切流中的剪切带（shear banding）现象。研究发现，当聚合物的平衡缠结数（equilibrium entanglement number）Z超过临界值Z_c时会发生剪切带，且该临界值依赖于约束释放（CCR）参数β。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用数值模拟方法研究聚合物在剪切流中的行为，并将结果与基于Rolie-Poly-like管动力学（tube dynamics）和对流约束释放（CCR）耦合的理论模型预测进行对比。CCR由参数β控制，其与弯曲刚度k_θ的依赖关系通过模拟计算得出。

Result: 理论模型预测当聚合物的平衡缠结数Z超过依赖于β的临界值Z_c时会发生剪切带。数值模拟结果与模型预测呈现半定量一致，偏差源于模型固有近似以及管模型在强流场中描述部分解缠结液体的不足。

Conclusion: 研究结果表明，数值模拟与理论模型在半定量层面具有一致性，有助于确定实际物理聚合物发生剪切带的条件。偏差揭示了管模型在强流场中描述部分解缠结体系的局限性。

Abstract: Results from numerical simulations of polymers under shear flow are compared with predictions for shear banding based on a model coupling Rolie-Poly-like tube dynamics to the entanglement dynamics mediated by Convected Constraint Release (CCR). CCR is controlled by a parameter $β$, whose dependence on the bending stiffness $k_θ$ is calculated from the simulations. The model predicts shear banding for polymers whose equilibrium entanglement number $Z$ exceeds a critical value $Z_{c}$ that depends on $β$. The simulations are in semi-quantitative agreement with the model, with deviations that are attributed to approximations inherent in the model, and the inadequacy of tube models to describe partially-disentangled liquids in strong flow. These results may help determine which physical polymers could undergo shear banding.

</details>

Abstract: We propose the use of an in-house air-filled elasto-bubble as a novel subwavelength acoustic resonator. Indeed, through experiments performed in an impedance tube, we observe a strong acoustic response and efficient transmission reduction, in good agreement with the theory considering a layered bubble introduced by Alekseev and Rybak (1999). ### [139] [Zero-temperature Avalanche Criticality Governing Dynamical Heterogeneity in Supercooled Liquids](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.03573)
*Norihiro Oyama,Yusuke Hara,Takeshi Kawasaki,Kang Kim*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究通过分子模拟（molecular simulations）表明，过冷液体（supercooled liquids）中动力学异质性（dynamical heterogeneity）的温度和系统尺寸依赖性可以用零温雪崩临界性（zero-temperature avalanche criticality）图像来解释。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 过冷液体中普遍存在介观尺度（mesoscale）的流动与非流动区域，即动力学异质性现象。虽然已知这些区域的特征尺寸随冷却而增大并表现出系统尺寸依赖性，但其物理起源仍是活跃的争论焦点。

Method: 研究采用分子模拟方法，在零温雪崩临界性框架下分析动力学异质性的温度和系统尺寸依赖性。

Result: 模拟结果表明，动力学异质性的温度依赖性和系统尺寸依赖性可以在零温雪崩临界性图像中得到统一解释。

Abstract: In supercooled liquids, mesoscale mobile and immobile domains are ubiquitously observed, a phenomenon known as dynamical heterogeneity. However, the physical origin of this domain growth remains a matter of active debate. In this work, using molecular simulations, we demonstrate that the temperature and system-size dependence of dynamical heterogeneity can be explained within a zero-temperature avalanche criticality picture.

### [140] [Potential energy landscape picture of zero-temperature avalanche criticality governing dynamics in supercooled liquids](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.03580)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过分子动力学模拟（molecular dynamics simulations），首先证明非平凡慢动力学可以用零温雪崩临界性图像描述。然后从三个不同角度量化势能景观（potential energy landscape），并基于这些分析提出雪崩临界性的势能景观图像。

Abstract: Supercooled liquids are metastable states realized by suppressing crystallization below the melting temperature. While it is well established that their dynamics slow down dramatically and become spatially heterogeneous upon cooling, the microscopic origin of these nontrivial glassy phenomena remains a matter of active debate. In the present study, by means of molecular dynamics simulations, we first demonstrate that nontrivial slow dynamics, such as structural relaxation and dynamical heterogeneity, can be consistently described within a zero-temperature avalanche criticality picture. Since this finding suggests that the potential energy landscape plays a crucial role in determining the dynamics, we further quantify the potential energy landscape from three distinct perspectives. Based on these analyses, we propose a potential-energy-landscape picture of avalanche criticality that is consistent with various previous studies. Our proposed picture explains in a unified manner previously unexplained observations near the mode-coupling transition, such as the saturation of the dynamical susceptibility and the localization of unstable modes in saddle configurations.

### [141] [Pre-yielding mechanical response near the jamming transition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.03651)
*Hidemasa Bessho,Takeshi Kawasaki,Kunimasa Miyazaki*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了接近堵塞转变点（jamming transition）的无摩擦颗粒体系在剪切应变下的力学响应，揭示了线性与非线性区域共存时的复杂粘弹性行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 堵塞态（jammed state）无摩擦颗粒体系在剪切应变下的力学和流变性质尚未被完全理解，特别是在应变幅值远低于屈服阈值时。体系在堵塞转变点（jamming transition point）φ_J 以上表现出两种异常的力学行为，本研究旨在探究这两种异常行为在 φ_J 附近共存区域的力学响应。

Method: 研究采用两种流变学协议（rheological protocols）进行数值分析：振荡剪切（oscillatory shear）和瞬态应力松弛（transient stress relaxation）。通过这两种方法探究接近堵塞转变点时体系的力学响应。

Result: 结果表明，力学响应并非简单地表现为两种代数弛豫（algebraic relaxations）的叠加。相反，体系在 φ_J 以上甚至以下都展现出丰富的非线性粘弹性行为（nonlinear viscoelastic behavior）。

Conclusion: 在接近堵塞转变点时，无摩擦颗粒体系的力学响应呈现出复杂的非线性粘弹性特征，无法用线性与非线性区域的简单叠加来描述，这深化了对堵塞体系流变行为的理解。

Abstract: The mechanical and rheological properties of jammed packings of frictionless particles under shear strain remain not fully understood, even when the strain amplitude is very small and well below the yielding threshold. Systems above the jamming transition point $φ_J$ are known to display two anomalous mechanical behaviors with respect to the driving frequency $ω$ (or time $t$) and the strain amplitude $γ$. In the linear-response regime ($γ\to 0$), the complex modulus exhibits an algebraic scaling, $G(ω)\simω^{1/2}$ (or $G(t)\sim t^{-1/2}$ in the time representation). In contrast, in the quasi-static limit ($ω\to 0$), the modulus shows the nonlinear behavior, $G(γ)\simγ^{-1/2}$, a phenomenon referred to as softening. The ranges of $ω$ and $γ$ over which these algebraic scalings hold broaden as $φ_J$ is approached from above, whereas both $G(ω)$ and $G(γ)$ vanish for $φ< φ_J$. In this study, we investigate the mechanical response in the regime where these two anomalies coexist in the vicinity of $φ_J$. To this end, we perform numerical analyses using two rheological protocols: oscillatory shear and transient stress relaxation. Our results demonstrate that the mechanical responses are not simply described as a superposition of the two algebraic relaxations and instead exhibit rich nonlinear viscoelastic behavior both above and even below $φ_J$.

Conclusion: 通过比较主要方法及其局限性，该综述概述了当前挑战，并展望了实现更预测性和高效的各向异性磁性胶体建模的前景，为未来研究提供了方向性指导。

Abstract: Anisotropic magnetic colloids with permanent dipole moments exhibit rich field-responsive behavior arising from the interplay between particle geometry, dipolar interactions, and external driving. Modeling these systems remains challenging due to the long-range nature of dipolar forces, geometric anisotropy, dipole--particle misalignment, and the complexity of implementing anisotropic steric interactions. This review discusses particle-based numerical strategies to model such systems, including single-site, multi-bead, shifted-dipole, and multicore representations. We analyze how different levels of description capture key physical mechanisms, from steric constraints and directional binding to internal magnetic structure and nonequilibrium dynamics. Particular emphasis is placed on dipole--particle misalignment as a control parameter that strongly affects interaction landscapes and self-assembly pathways. We also highlight recent machine learning approaches as emerging tools to construct effective interaction potentials and accelerate simulations. By comparing the main methodologies and their limitations, this review outlines current challenges and perspectives toward more predictive and efficient modeling of anisotropic magnetic colloids.

Abstract: Understanding thermal fluctuations yields insights into a wide range of behaviors in many-body systems. Conclusion: 该工作建立了一种高度可编程的分子工程策略，能够瓦解声子气模型（phonon gas model），迫使晶体框架进入极端扩散输运区域（extreme diffusive transport regime）。柔性侧链使载热声子模式（heat-carrying phonon modes）受到临界阻尼，其平均自由程严格限制在纳米尺度，寿命坍缩至Ioffe-Regel极限。

Abstract: While crystalline materials with glass-like thermal conductivity are fundamentally intriguing, structurally triggering the transition from propagating to diffusive heat transport within a single framework remains a formidable challenge. Here, using extensive machine learning molecular dynamics, we demonstrate a fundamental thermal transport crossover in metal-organic frameworks. We reveal that grafting flexible side chains onto a pristine MOF backbone acts as a structural switch, strongly reducing the thermal conductivity by $\sim$70% (from $\sim 0.7$ to $\sim 0.2\ \text{W m}^{-1}\text{K}^{-1}$ at 300 K). Crucially, the functionalized derivatives exhibit a drastic transition from a classical Peierls $\sim 1/T$ decay to an anomalous, temperature-independent glass-like plateau. Reciprocal- and real-space analyses reveal the microscopic origins: the side chains act as built-in local resonators that trap acoustic energy via strong low-frequency resonant hybridization, while simultaneously inducing extreme steric crowding. Consequently, the heat-carrying phonon modes become critically damped, with their mean free paths strictly confined to the nanometer scale and their lifetimes collapsing to the Ioffe-Regel limit. This work establishes a highly programmable molecular engineering strategy to dismantle the phonon gas model, forcing crystalline frameworks into an extreme diffusive transport regime.

*Michio Otsuki,Kiwamu Yoshii,Hideyuki Mizuno*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 剪切模量在压缩-解压过程中表现出显著的滞后现象，尽管粒子间力定律本身是历史无关的。对于纯排斥性颗粒，当以压力表征力学性质时滞后消失，但在黏性堆积中持续存在，表明压力不是黏性颗粒的唯一状态变量。扩展的EMT显示剪切模量的函数形式对排斥性和黏性颗粒相同，但吸引相互作用破坏了边际稳定性（marginal stability）。

Abstract: The dependence of mechanical properties on microscopic interactions remains a central problem in the physics of disordered solids near the jamming transition. We numerically and theoretically investigate the mechanical response of jammed cohesive granular materials using discrete element simulations and effective medium theory (EMT). We find that the shear modulus exhibits pronounced hysteresis under compression and decompression, even though the interparticle force law itself is strictly history-independent. While such hysteresis disappears for purely repulsive particles when mechanical properties are characterized in terms of pressure, it persists in cohesive packings, indicating that pressure is not a unique state variable for cohesive particles. Extending EMT to cohesive interactions, we show that the functional form of the shear modulus remains the same for both repulsive and cohesive particles, but that attractive interactions violate marginal stability. The resulting deviation from marginal stability generates excess rigidity, as predicted by a scaling relation. This prediction is quantitatively verified by numerical simulations and explains the persistent hysteresis in cohesive packings.

### [146] [On the Optimality of Reduced-Order Models for Band Structure Computations: A Kolmogorov $n$-Width Perspective](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.04338)
*Ankit Srivastava*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 利用Kolmogorov n-宽度概念，基于Bloch变换算符的解析性和Kato解析微扰理论，分析解流形的逼近性质；对于能带簇，采用谱投影算子而非单个特征向量来处理内部交叉。

Result: 解流形的Kolmogorov n-宽度以指数衰减，衰减率由感兴趣能带与其相邻能带之间的最小能隙控制；对于能带簇，只有簇与剩余谱之间的能隙才影响衰减率。

Conclusion: 结果为任何线性降阶方法的误差提供了尖锐下界，可用于衡量现有方法；数值实验证实了预测的指数衰减，并表明贪婪算法能达到接近最优的收敛性。

Abstract: In this paper, we exploit the concept of Kolmogorov $n$-widths to establish optimality benchmarks for reduced-order methods used in phononic, acoustic, and photonic band structure calculations. The Bloch-transformed operators are entire holomorphic functions of the wave vector~$\kk$, and by Kato's analytic perturbation theory the eigenpairs inherit this holomorphy wherever the spectral gap is positive. The Kolmogorov $n$-width of the solution manifold therefore decays exponentially, at a rate controlled by the minimum spectral gap between the band of interest and its neighbors. For clusters of bands, we show that working with spectral projectors rather than individual eigenvectors renders all internal crossings -- avoided, symmetry-enforced, or conical -- irrelevant: only the gap separating the cluster from the remaining spectrum matters. These results provide a sharp lower bound on the error of any linear reduction method, against which existing approaches can be measured. Numerical experiments on one- and two-dimensional problems confirm the predicted exponential decay and demonstrate that a greedy algorithm achieves near-optimal convergence. It also provides a principled justification for the choice of basis vectors in highly successful reduced-order models like RBME.

### [147] [Breaking the Entanglement-Structure Trade-off: Many-Body Localization Protects Emergent Holographic Geometry in Random Tensor Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.04596)
*Zhihua Liang*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 该研究通过随机张量网络（RTN）系统性地探索了"纠缠几何引力"链，验证了运动学基础并发现多体局域化（MBL）是保护涌现全息几何免于热化的机制。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 研究确认了运动学基础（斜率=1.000，相关性=0.92，局域性3.3倍），但引力动力学（JT引力）未涌现。发现无序强度W_c≈10-12处存在有限尺寸交叉，当W>W_c时互信息-晶格相关性持续存在。最优参数区域为近伊辛各向异性Δ≈50且W=30，相关性r=0.779±0.002。MBL保护纠缠的空间结构而非总量，打破了量子单调性施加的纠缠结构权衡。

Conclusion: 多体局域化（MBL）是保护涌现全息几何免于热化的关键机制，它能够维持纠缠的空间结构。只有全息（RTN）初始态能够维持几何，而积态、Néel态和Bell对态则不能。MBL独特地打破了量子单调性施加的纠缠结构权衡。

Abstract: We present a systematic numerical investigation of the "entanglement geometry gravity" chain in random tensor networks (RTN) established by the ER EPR conjecture and Jacobson's thermodynamic derivation. First, we verify the kinematic foundation: the entanglement first law $δ\langle K\rangle=δS$ (slope=1.000), the encoding of geometry by mutual information (correlation=0.92), and the locality of holographic perturbations (3.3x). We also confirm that gravitational dynamics (JT gravity) does not emerge, identifying a sharp kinematics-dynamics boundary. Second, and more importantly, we discover that many-body localization (MBL) is the mechanism that protects emergent holographic geometry from thermalization. Replacing Haar-random evolution (geometry lifetime $t\sim6$) with an XXZ Hamiltonian plus on-site disorder, we observe a finite-size crossover at disorder strength $W_c\approx10-12$ above which mutual-information-lattice correlations persist indefinitely ($r>0.5$ for $t>50$). We map the full parameter space: the optimal regime is a near-Ising anisotropy $Δ\approx50$ with $W=30$ yielding $r=0.779\pm0.002$ (confirmed by a fine scan over $Δ\in[30,70]$); only holographic (RTN) initial states sustain geometry, while product, Néel, and Bell-pair states do not. MBL preserves the spatial structure of entanglement (adjacent/non-adjacent MI ratio ~2.6-4.2x vs. 1.0x in the thermal phase), rather than its total amount. A comparison with classical cellular automata reveals that MBL uniquely breaks the entanglement-structure trade-off imposed by quantum monogamy: classical systems achieve spatial structure only at the cost of negligible mutual information, while MBL sustains both.

### [148] [A solvable model of noisy coupled oscillators with fully random interactions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.04404)
*Harukuni Ikeda*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文引入了一个具有完全随机相互作用和分布自然频率的可解球形耦合振子模型，研究了自然频率分布如何抑制有限温度自旋玻璃转变，同时发现零温度下玻璃相仍然存在。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究耦合振子系统在非平衡扰动下的玻璃化行为，特别是自然频率分布如何影响自旋玻璃转变，为理解非平衡条件下玻璃态冻结的抑制机制提供可解的理论框架。

Method: 采用动力学平均场理论（dynamical mean-field theory），推导了稳态响应函数和相关函数的自洽方程，分析了球形约束条件下自然频率分布宽度对系统行为的影响。

Result: 任何有限宽度的自然频率分布都会抑制有限温度自旋玻璃转变，因为相关函数的低频奇异性与球形约束不兼容；然而在零温度下，任意频率色散下玻璃相仍然存在。

Conclusion: 该模型为研究非平衡扰动如何抑制有限温度玻璃态冻结提供了可解的振子框架，但零温度下的残余玻璃性可能是球形动力学的特殊特征，会被局部非线性破坏。

Abstract: We introduce a solvable spherical model of coupled oscillators with fully random interactions and distributed natural frequencies. Using the dynamical mean-field theory, we derive self-consistent equations for the steady-state response and correlation functions. We show that any finite width of the natural-frequency distribution suppresses the finite-temperature spin-glass transition, because the resulting low-frequency singularity of the correlation function is incompatible with the spherical constraint. At zero temperature, however, a spin-glass phase persists for arbitrary frequency dispersion. This residual zero-temperature glassiness is likely a special feature of the spherical dynamics and would be destroyed by local nonlinearities. The model thus provides a solvable oscillator framework for studying how nonequilibrium perturbations suppress finite-temperature glassy freezing.

</details>


### [149] [The Bott Metric: A Real-Space Bridge Between Topology and Quantum Metric](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.04447)
*Kaustav Chatterjee,Ronika Sarkar,Md Afsar Reja,Awadhesh Narayan*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 该论文引入并发展了Bott度量（Bott metric），作为Bott指数的补充工具，用于捕获系统的量子度量结构，特别适用于非周期系统。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Bott指数已成为探测量子物质拓扑性质的重要工具，特别是在缺乏平移对称性的系统中。然而，Bott指数仅保留相位信息而丢弃振幅信息，需要一种能够捕获互补振幅信息的度量工具。

Method: 论文引入并发展了Bott度量，该度量基于plaquette算子构造，能够捕获Bott指数所丢弃的振幅信息。该方法提供了揭示非周期系统中量子度量结构的新途径。

Result: 研究显示，在热力学极限下，Bott度量收敛于积分量子度量的迹（trace of the integrated quantum metric）。通过从无序到非晶模型（amorphous models）的代表性示例，验证了该框架的有效性。

Conclusion: Bott度量的定义在相同的plaquette算子构造下统一了拓扑不变量（topological invariants）和量子度量的概念，为研究非周期系统的量子度量结构提供了新框架。

Abstract: The Bott index has become an indispensable tool to probe the topology of quantum matter, particularly in systems lacking translational symmetry. Constructed from a plaquette operator, it retains the phase information while discarding the amplitude. Here we introduce and develop the Bott metric, which captures this complementary amplitude information and provides a measure of the underlying quantum metric of the system. We show that, in the thermodynamic limit, the Bott metric converges to the trace of the integrated quantum metric. Our framework provides a new route to reveal the quantum metric structure in non-periodic systems, which we illustrate using representative examples ranging from disordered to amorphous models. More broadly, our definition of the Bott metric unifies the notion of topological invariants and quantum metric under the same overarching plaquette operator construction.

</details>


### [150] [Interpretation of Crystal Energy Landscapes with Kolmogorov-Arnold Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.04636)
*Gen Zu,Ning Mao,Claudia Felser,Yang Zhang*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 该论文引入可解释的Kolmogorov-Arnold网络（KANs）作为材料信息学新框架，通过元素加权KAN模型在预测形成能、带隙和功函数方面达到最先进精度，同时无需显式物理约束即可揭示与元素周期表和量子力学原理一致的可解释化学趋势。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 表征晶体能量景观对于预测热力学稳定性、电子结构和功能行为至关重要。虽然机器学习（ML）能够实现快速性质预测，但大多数模型的"黑箱"特性限制了其生成新科学见解的效用。

Method: 引入Kolmogorov-Arnold网络（KANs）作为可解释框架，与具有固定激活函数的传统神经网络不同，KANs采用可学习函数来揭示潜在的物理关系。开发了元素加权KAN（Element-Weighted KAN），这是一个仅基于成分的模型。

Result: 元素加权KAN在大规模数据集上预测形成能（formation energy）、带隙（band gap）和功函数（work function）方面达到了最先进的精度。重要的是，无需任何显式物理约束，通过嵌入分析、相关性研究和主成分分析（principal component analysis），KANs揭示了与元素周期表和量子力学原理一致的可解释化学趋势。

Conclusion: KANs提供了一个具有高预测性能和科学可解释性的强大框架，为透明、基于化学的材料信息学建立了新范式（new paradigm）。

Abstract: Characterizing crystalline energy landscapes is essential to predicting thermodynamic stability, electronic structure, and functional behavior. While machine learning (ML) enables rapid property predictions, the "black-box" nature of most models limits their utility for generating new scientific insights. Here, we introduce Kolmogorov-Arnold Networks (KANs) as an interpretable framework to bridge this gap. Unlike conventional neural networks with fixed activation functions, KANs employ learnable functions that reveal underlying physical relationships. We developed the Element-Weighted KAN, a composition-only model that achieves state-of-the-art accuracy in predicting formation energy, band gap, and work function across large-scale datasets. Crucially, without any explicit physical constraints, KANs uncover interpretable chemical trends aligned with the periodic table and quantum mechanical principles through embedding analysis, correlation studies, and principal component analysis. These results demonstrate that KANs provide a powerful framework with high predictive performance and scientific interpretability, establishing a new paradigm for transparent, chemistry-based materials informatics.

### [151] [Scaling atom-by-atom inverse design with nano-topology optimization and diffusion models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.03276)
*Chun-Teh Chen,Denvid Lau*

Main category: physics.app-ph

TL;DR: 本文开发了一种原子级逆向设计框架，将纳米拓扑优化（Nano-TO）与条件去噪扩散概率模型相结合，用于金属纳米结构的力学性能优化。该框架揭示了表面物理驱动的拓扑选择规则，并证明在纳米尺度下原子级优化优于连续介质拓扑优化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 金属纳米结构的力学性能不仅受拓扑结构影响，还受晶体对称性和面特异性表面物理（face-specific surface physics）的调控，而这些因素在传统的连续介质拓扑优化（continuum topology optimization）中通常被忽略。因此需要开发能够考虑原子级特征的逆向设计方法。

Method: 开发了原子级逆向设计框架，结合了纳米拓扑优化（Nano-Topology Optimization, Nano-TO）与条件去噪扩散概率模型（conditional denoising diffusion probabilistic models）。Nano-TO将每个原子视为离散设计变量，通过总能量对称曲率（symmetric curvature of the total energy）评估刚度，消除残余表面应力偏差（residual surface-stress bias）。采用晶体学对齐的多壳层灵敏度滤波器（crystallography-aligned multi-shell sensitivity filter）稳定优化过程。

Result: 在铝纳米悬臂梁（aluminum nanocantilevers）研究中，发现了表面物理驱动的拓扑选择规则：厚度周期性梁倾向于支撑主导的桁架结构（brace-dominated trusses），而有限厚度梁则偏好近乎封闭的壁结构，提供有效的剪切路径并减少表面惩罚。在纳米尺度足够小时，这些壁结构变得力学不稳定，桁架状布局重新出现。纳米柱（nanopillar）研究表明，原子级优化设计优于连续介质拓扑优化设计。基于Nano-TO数据训练的条件扩散模型能够在优化前沿附近生成多样化的高性能候选结构。

Conclusion: 研究结果表明，纳米尺度逆向设计是拓扑结构与表面物理耦合的问题。所开发的原子级设计框架能够有效考虑晶体对称性和表面物理效应，为金属纳米结构的力学性能优化提供了新方法。

Abstract: The mechanical properties of metallic nanostructures are governed not only by topology but also by crystal symmetry and face-specific surface physics, which are typically absent from continuum topology optimization. We develop an atom-by-atom inverse design framework that combines Nano-Topology Optimization (Nano-TO) with conditional denoising diffusion probabilistic models. Nano-TO treats each atom as a discrete design variable and evaluates stiffness from the symmetric curvature of the total energy, removing residual surface-stress bias. A crystallography-aligned multi-shell sensitivity filter stabilizes the optimization and enables designs containing more than 6.5 x 10^5 atoms. Using aluminum nanocantilevers, we identify a surface-physics-driven topology selection rule: thickness-periodic beams favor brace-dominated trusses, whereas finite-thickness beams favor nearly closed walls that provide efficient shear paths and reduce surface penalties. At sufficiently small scales, these walls become mechanically unstable, and truss-like layouts reappear. In nanopillar studies, atomistic optimization outperforms continuum topology-optimized designs. Finally, conditional diffusion models trained on Nano-TO data generate diverse high-performance candidates near the optimization frontier. These results establish nanoscale inverse design as a coupled problem of topology and surface physics.

</details>

*Thomas Beckers,Leonardo Colombo*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 本文结合高斯过程分布式端口哈密顿系统（GP-dPHS）学习与边界控制互联（boundary control by interconnection）。GP-dPHS模型用于从数据中推断未知的哈密顿结构，同时其后验不确定性被纳入基于能量的鲁棒性分析中。

Result: 该方法得出了概率性条件，即使在模型失配的情况下，也能保证闭环轨迹保持有界。该方法在模拟的浅水系统（shallow water system）中得到了验证。

Conclusion: 通过将数据驱动的哈密顿结构学习与基于能量的鲁棒性分析相结合，该方法为处理具有不确定性的物理系统控制问题提供了一种有效途径。

Abstract: Distributed Port-Hamiltonian (dPHS) theory provides a powerful framework for modeling physical systems governed by partial differential equations and has enabled a broad class of boundary control methodologies. Their effectiveness, however, relies heavily on the availability of accurate system models, which may be difficult to obtain in the presence of nonlinear and partially unknown dynamics. To address this challenge, we combine Gaussian Process distributed Port-Hamiltonian system (GP-dPHS) learning with boundary control by interconnection. The GP-dPHS model is used to infer the unknown Hamiltonian structure from data, while its posterior uncertainty is incorporated into an energy-based robustness analysis. This yields probabilistic conditions under which the closed-loop trajectories remain bounded despite model mismatch. The method is illustrated on a simulated shallow water system.

### [153] [Non-reciprocal Ising gauge theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.03367)
*Nilotpal Chakraborty,Anton Souslov,Claudio Castelnovo*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了非互易性（non-reciprocity）与几何阻挫（geometric frustration）在伊辛规范理论（Ising gauge theory）中的相互作用，揭示了其导致的新型结构、动力学现象及准粒子约束效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在探索非互易性与几何阻挫的相互作用如何超越各自单独效应，在多体系统中产生更丰富的结构及动力学现象，从而避免晶体有序并展现复杂液体行为。

Method: 构建了一个最小模型，其中两个伊辛规范理论副本以非互易方式耦合，关键保留了局域$\mathbb{Z}_2$对称性。通过分析组合威尔逊环观测量（combined Wilson loop observable）及准粒子动力学来研究系统行为。

Result: 发现组合威尔逊环观测量呈现线性渐近标度，准粒子对约束长度由非互易耦合强度调节。单个退局域激发因非互易性诱导的强相互作用，在临界渗流簇上遵循自回避轨迹运动，导致拓扑对数贡献及准粒子陷获产生的长寿命亚稳态。

Conclusion: 非互易性与几何阻挫的相互作用产生了超越各自单独效应的丰富现象，包括可调节的准粒子约束、临界动力学行为及拓扑特征，为几何阻挫非互易性的更广泛研究开辟了道路。

Abstract: Non-reciprocity and geometric frustration enable many-body systems to avoid crystalline order and instead exhibit complex, liquid-like behavior. Here we show that their interplay is richer than the sum of its parts, leading to surprising structural and dynamical phenomena. In our minimal model, two copies of Ising gauge theory are non-reciprocally coupled in a way that crucially preserves a local $\mathbb{Z}_2$ symmetry. We discover that the combined Wilson loop observable of the two copies exhibits linear asymptotic scaling, with a quasiparticle-pair confinement length tuned by the strength of the non-reciprocal coupling. Key dynamical features are revealed in the behavior of individual deconfined excitations due to strong interactions induced by the non-reciprocity, leading to motion on a critical percolation cluster that follows a self-avoiding trail. Mapping from this quasiparticle dynamics onto the magnetic noise spectrum, we discover that non-reciprocity tunes topological logarithmic contributions and causes long-lived metastable states due to quasiparticle trapping. Our work opens the way for broader investigations of geometrically frustrated non-reciprocity.

### [154] [Random matrix theory of integrability-to-chaos transition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.03669)
*Ben Craps,Marine De Clerck,Oleg Evnin,Maxim Pavlov*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种随机矩阵系综（random matrix ensemble），能够准确描述可积与混沌系统过渡区的能级间距分布，并发现微扰哈密顿量矩阵元分布具有普适的幂律特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子能级间距统计是研究量子混沌（quantum chaos）与量子可积性（quantum integrability）的关键判据。虽然完全可积与完全混沌系统对应的分布具有普适性（分别为泊松分布与维格纳-戴森分布），但可积与混沌过渡区的分布缺乏普适性且尚未被定量理解。

Method: 研究指出，控制这些分布的关键统计量是未受扰可积系统能量本征基下非可积微扰哈密顿量（nonintegrable perturbation Hamiltonian）的矩阵元统计。基于这一洞见，构建了一个简单的随机矩阵系综（random matrix ensemble）。

Result: 该随机矩阵系综能够正确复现多种测试系统中的能级间距分布。此外，研究发现构建中涉及的矩阵元分布展现出惊人的普适特征：在不同物理系统中，这些分布由简单的幂律（power laws）主导。

Conclusion: 研究揭示了可积-混沌过渡区能级统计的定量描述方法，并发现了微扰矩阵元分布的普适幂律行为，为理解量子混沌与可积性之间的过渡提供了新框架。

Abstract: The statistics of gaps between quantum energy levels is a hallmark criterion in quantum chaos and quantum integrability studies. The relevant distributions corresponding to exactly integrable vs. fully chaotic systems are universal and described by the Poisson vs. Wigner-Dyson curves. In the transitional regime between integrability and chaos, the distributions are much less universal and have not been understood quantitatively until now. We point out that the relevant statistics that controls these distributions is that of the matrix elements of the nonintegrable perturbation Hamiltonian in the energy eigenbasis of the unperturbed integrable system. With this insight, we formulate a simple random matrix ensemble that correctly reproduces the level spacing distributions in a variety of test systems. For the distribution of matrix elements appearing in our construction, we furthermore discover surprising universal features: across a variety of physical systems with diverse degrees of freedom, these distributions are dominated by simple power laws.

</details>


### [155] [Geometry- and topology-controlled synchronization phase transition on manifolds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.03770)
*Yang Tian*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究将Kuramoto-Sakaguchi模型从球面推广到任意维度的紧致、连通、可定向齐次黎曼流形，揭示了流形几何与拓扑如何共同塑造同步相变：几何控制临界耦合系数，拓扑通过欧拉示性数约束相变类型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在探索底层流形的几何与拓扑如何影响系统的同步相变（synchronization phase transition）。通过将Kuramoto-Sakaguchi模型从球面推广到更一般的流形，可以系统分析几何和拓扑因素在相变过程中的作用。

Method: 方法包括：将Kuramoto-Sakaguchi模型扩展到任意维度的紧致、连通、可定向齐次黎曼流形（compact, connected, orientable, and homogeneous Riemannian manifolds）；从流形上的平均场动力学方程出发，推导非相干态附近序参量的局部响应方程；分离几何和拓扑对相变的贡献。

Result: 研究发现：流形几何通过系数κ(M)控制非相干态线性失稳的临界耦合；流形拓扑通过欧拉示性数χ(M)约束响应方程的三次项。当χ(M)≠0时，拓扑不允许一般的连续或三临界同步相变，并对初始有序纹理施加非零净缺陷电荷。当χ(M)=0时，拓扑不施加这种阻碍，允许连续、不连续和三临界局部分支。

Conclusion: 该框架恢复了经典的超球面宇称定律（hyperspherical parity law）并将其扩展到广泛的非球面状态空间，包括超球面、偶维球积、复格拉斯曼流形、复射影空间、平坦环面、实Stiefel流形、旋转群和酉群等代表性流形族。

Abstract: In this work, we explore how the geometry and topology of the underlying manifold shape the synchronization phase transition of a system. To do so, we extend the Kuramoto-Sakaguchi model from spheres to compact, connected, orientable, and homogeneous Riemannian manifolds of arbitrary dimension. Starting from the mean-field kinetic equation on the manifold, we derive a local response equation for the order parameter near the incoherent state and separate the geometric and topological contributions to the phase transition out of the incoherent state. The manifold geometry determines a coefficient $κ\left(M\right)$ to control the critical coupling for the linear loss of stability of the incoherent state. The manifold topology constrains the cubic term of the response equation through the Euler characteristic $χ\left(M\right)$. Under a local sign condition on the cubic term, topology does not allow a generic continuous or tricritical synchronization phase transition to occur when $χ\left(M\right)\neq 0$, and it imposes a non-zero net defect charge on the incipient ordered texture. When an additional local stabilization condition holds in that nonzero-Euler class, topology further selects a discontinuous phase transition. When $χ\left(M\right)=0$, topology does not impose that obstruction, so continuous, discontinuous, and tricritical local branches are all allowed. We verify these findings on representative families including hyperspheres, equal even-sphere products, complex Grassmannians, complex projective spaces, flat tori, real Stiefel manifolds, rotation groups, and unitary groups. Our framework recovers the classical hyperspherical parity law and extends it to a broad class of non-spherical state spaces.

</details>


### [156] [Statistics of Matrix Elements of Operators in a Disorder-Free SYK model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.03977)
*Tingfei Li,Shuanghong Li*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文研究了无序自由SYK模型中非对角矩阵元素的统计特性，发现其服从广义逆高斯分布而非Fréchet分布，为特征态热化假说提供了新的理论依据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 先前研究表明Lieb-Liniger模型中非对角矩阵元素的概率分布函数可由Fréchet分布良好描述，这对特征态热化假说（Eigenstate Thermalization Hypothesis, ETH）具有重要意义。本文旨在探究另一可解模型——无序自由Sachdev-Ye-Kitaev（SYK）模型中是否出现类似现象。

Method: 研究采用无序自由SYK模型，其哈密顿量由Majorana费米子的四体相互作用构成，耦合强度固定为常数。评估由n个Majorana费米子乘积构成的算符矩阵元素：$\mathcal{O} = χ_{a_1}χ_{a_2}\ldots χ_{a_n}$，分析其非对角矩阵元素的统计特性。

Result: 对于一般指标选择且$n \geq 4$的情况，研究发现非对角矩阵元素的统计特性可由广义逆高斯分布（generalized inverse Gaussian distribution）良好拟合，而非Fréchet分布。

Conclusion: 无序自由SYK模型中非对角矩阵元素的统计分布呈现与Lieb-Liniger模型不同的特征，服从广义逆高斯分布而非Fréchet分布，这为特征态热化假说在不同可解模型中的表现提供了新的理论视角。

Abstract: Recently, studies have explored the statistics of matrix elements of local operators in the Lieb-Liniger model. It was found that the probability distribution function for off-diagonal matrix elements $\langle \boldsymbolμ|\mathcal{O}|\boldsymbolλ \rangle$ within the same macro-state is well described by the Fréchet distributions. This represents a significant development for the Eigenstate Thermalization Hypothesis (ETH). In this paper, we investigate a similar phenomenon in another solvable model: the disorder-free Sachdev-Ye-Kitaev (SYK) model. The Hamiltonian of this model consists of 4-body interactions of Majorana fermions. Unlike the conventional SYK model, the coupling strengths in this model are fixed to a constant, earning it the name ``disorder-free.'' We evaluate the matrix elements of operators constructed from products of $n$ Majorana fermions: $\mathcal{O} = χ_{a_1}χ_{a_2}\ldots χ_{a_n}$. For a general choice of indices and $n \geq 4$, we find that the statistics of the off-diagonal matrix elements are well-fitted by a generalized inverse Gaussian distribution rather than Fréchet distributions.

### [158] [Cross Spectra Break the Single-Channel Impossibility](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.03775)
*Yuda Bi,Vince D Calhoun*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该论文证明，通过引入第二个观测通道（second observed channel），可以克服单通道高斯时间序列无法检测时间不可逆性的限制。交叉谱（cross-spectral）结构提供了全新的可检测性，将可观测的交叉谱结构与系统耗散联系起来。
