  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Lucente等人证明，对于来自线性系统的标量高斯时间序列（scalar Gaussian time series），任何时间不可逆性度量（time-irreversibility measure）都无法检测其偏离平衡态。本研究旨在探索如何克服这一不可能性，通过引入额外的观测通道来检测系统的时间不可逆性。

Method: 采用双通道观测方法，引入共享相同隐藏驱动器的第二个观测通道。通过分析交叉谱块（cross-spectral block）结构，该结构在单通道度量中无法访问。研究聚焦于交叉谱可检测性系数$\Scross$，该系数在零假设下表现出独特的独立性特征。

Result: 交叉谱可检测性系数$\Scross$在零假设下精确独立于观测时间尺度，仅由隐藏模式参数决定。在精确时间尺度合并处，所有单通道度量消失时，$\Scross$保持严格正值。对于单向耦合的Ornstein-Uhlenbeck系统，熵产生率（entropy production rate, EPR）满足$\EPRtot=α_2λ^2$的精确关系，且$\Scross>0$证明$\EPRtot>0$。

Conclusion: 交叉谱占据谱矩阵（spectral matrix）的非对角线子空间，与任何对角线零假设正交，因此在任何单通道约化中不可见。可观测的交叉谱结构与全系统耗散通过$\EPRtot^{\,2}\propto\Scross$关系相联系，为双胶体探针和多站点气候站的定量检测阈值分裂提供了理论基础。

Abstract: Lucente et al. proved that no time-irreversibility measure can detect departure from equilibrium in a scalar Gaussian time series from a linear system. We show that a second observed channel sharing the same hidden driver overcomes this impossibility: the cross-spectral block, structurally inaccessible to any single-channel measure, provides qualitatively new detectability. Under the diagonal null hypothesis, the cross-spectral detectability coefficient $\Scross$ (the leading quartic-order cross contribution) is \emph{exactly} independent of the observed timescales -- a cancellation governed solely by hidden-mode parameters -- and remains strictly positive at exact timescale coalescence, where all single-channel measures vanish. The mechanism is geometric: the cross spectrum occupies the off-diagonal subspace of the spectral matrix, orthogonal to any diagonal null and therefore invisible in any single-channel reduction. For the one-way coupled Ornstein--Uhlenbeck counterpart, the entropy production rate (EPR) satisfies $\EPRtot=α_2λ^2$ exactly; under this coupling geometry, $\Scross>0$ certifies $\EPRtot>0$, linking observable cross-spectral structure to full-system dissipation via $\EPRtot^{\,2}\propto\Scross$. Finite-sample simulations predict a quantitative detection-threshold split testable with dual colloidal probes and multisite climate stations.

### [159] [The Roaming Bethe Roots: An Effective Bethe Ansatz Beyond Integrability](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.04627)
*Wenlong Zhao,Yunfeng Jiang,Rui-Dong Zhu*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种有效的贝特拟设（effective Bethe ansatz）方法，用于求解近可积（near-integrable）量子多体系统。该方法通过重整化贝特根（renormalizing Bethe roots）来考虑可积性破缺（integrability-breaking）相互作用，为近可积模型的本征态提供了新的表示形式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子多体系统在可积点附近的研究具有重要意义，但传统贝特拟设（Bethe ansatz）方法无法直接处理可积性破缺（integrability-breaking）相互作用。需要发展一种能够保留可积性代数结构同时考虑非可积效应的近似方法。

Method: 提出有效的贝特拟设（effective Bethe ansatz），保留贝特波函数的函数形式，但通过重整化贝特根（renormalizing Bethe roots）来考虑可积性破缺相互作用。这些有效根通过最小化物理动机的成本函数（cost functions）来确定，产生的离壳贝特态（off-shell Bethe states）作为非可积模型的近似本征态。

Result: 测试表明，对于弱可积性破缺（weak integrability-breaking）模型，该方法在广泛的变形参数范围内提供了高质量的本征态近似。而对于强可积性破缺（strong integrability-breaking）模型，方法的有效性随变形参数增加而快速下降。该方法的效果可作为表征可积性破缺强度的有用探针。

Conclusion: 有效的贝特拟设为近可积模型的本征态提供了新的表示形式，使其能够利用从可积性继承的代数结构。该方法在准确度范围内为研究近可积量子多体系统提供了有效的理论工具。

Abstract: We propose an effective Bethe ansatz for solving quantum many-body systems near an integrable point. Our approach retains the functional form of the Bethe wave function while renormalizing the Bethe roots to account for integrability-breaking interactions. These effective roots are determined by minimizing physically motivated cost functions. The resulting off-shell Bethe states serve as approximate eigenstates of the non-integrable models. We assess the quality of the approximation using various physical observables, including the energy eigenvalue, state fidelity, and bipartite entanglement entropy. Our tests show that for models with weak integrability-breaking, the effective Bethe ansatz provides a high-quality approximation to the exact eigenstates over a wide range of deformation parameters. In contrast, for models with strong integrability-breaking interactions, the efficacy of the effective Bethe ansatz degrades relatively quickly as the deformation parameter increases. The efficacy of the method thus offers a useful probe for characterizing the strength of integrability breaking. Within its regime of accuracy, it also provides a new representation of the eigenstates of nearly integrable models, enabling one to exploit the algebraic structure inherited from integrability.

Abstract: This work presents a comprehensive benchmark and validation of a recently proposed method called Effective Bethe Ansatz (EBA). It is a variational method that deforms the exact Bethe wavefunctions of one-dimensional spin chains at integrable points to approximate non-integrable systems. We apply this method to the non-integrable regime of the spin-1 bilinear-biquadratic chain. By performing EBA method starting from the two integrable endpoints, the Takhtajan-Babujian point and the Lai-Sutherland point, we systematically evaluate the accuracy of the EBA for the ground state and first excited state. Our validation is based on a direct comparison with exact diagonalization, assessing energy, fidelity, and entanglement entropy. The results confirm that the EBA provides a physically accurate description near integrability, with fidelity decreasing controllably as the perturbation increases. The method successfully captures key finite-size effects, such as level crossings, manifested as sharp drops in fidelity, and provides a probe to potential phase transitions. This study establishes the EBA as a reliable and efficient semi-analytical tool, clarifying its scope and limitations for studying low-energy physics in non-integrable quantum spin chains.

This work demonstrates the rich dynamics underlying the thermalization process, and advances our understanding on the dynamical adaptations of many-body systems to external disturbances.

### [162] [Non-Equilibrium Stochastic Dynamics as a Unified Framework for Insight and Repetitive Learning: A Kramers Escape Approach to Continual Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.04154)
*Gunn Kim*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该论文从非平衡统计物理角度，为持续学习（continual learning）中的稳定性-可塑性困境（stability-plasticity dilemma）提供了统一理论框架。通过将学习系统建模为双势阱能量景观中的朗之万动力学粒子，揭示了弹性权重固化（EWC）惩罚项如何导致可塑性指数级崩溃，并区分了顿悟（insight）与重复学习（repetitive practice）的两种不同温度机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 持续学习在人工神经网络中面临稳定性-可塑性困境的根本限制：保留先验知识的系统往往抵制新知识获取，反之亦然。现有方法（如弹性权重固化）缺乏对可塑性随任务累积而崩溃的物理解释，同时顿悟与重复技能习得之间也缺乏统一的理论描述。

Method: 采用非平衡统计物理框架，将学习系统状态建模为在双势阱能量景观（double-well energy landscape）下演化的粒子，服从朗之万动力学（Langevin dynamics）。概率密度遵循福克-普朗克方程（Fokker-Planck equation），状态间转换由克莱默斯逃逸率（Kramers escape rate）描述，其中噪声振幅由时间依赖的有效温度T(t)控制。

Result: 研究取得两项主要贡献：首先，识别出弹性权重固化惩罚项作为能量壁垒，其高度随累积任务数量线性增长，导致转换率指数级崩溃，这一预测得到解析和数值验证。其次，表明顿悟与重复学习对应同一福克-普朗克方程中的两种不同温度协议：顿悟事件产生T(t)的瞬态尖峰驱动快速壁垒跨越，而重复学习在适度升高但固定的温度下运行，通过持续随机扩散实现转换。

Conclusion: 该研究建立了基于物理的框架来理解持续学习系统中的可塑性及其失效机制，为人工智能中自适应噪声调度（adaptive noise schedules）提供了原则性设计标准。通过统一描述顿悟与重复学习，为理解学习动态提供了新的理论基础。

Abstract: Continual learning in artificial neural networks is fundamentally limited by the stability--plasticity dilemma: systems that retain prior knowledge tend to resist acquiring new knowledge, and vice versa. Existing approaches, most notably elastic weight consolidation~(EWC), address this empirically without a physical account of why plasticity eventually collapses as tasks accumulate. Separately, the distinction between sudden insight and gradual skill acquisition through repetitive practice has lacked a unified theoretical description. Here, we show that both problems admit a common resolution within non-equilibrium statistical physics. We model the state of a learning system as a particle evolving under Langevin dynamics on a double-well energy landscape, with the noise amplitude governed by a time-dependent effective temperature $T(t)$. The probability density obeys a Fokker--Planck equation, and transitions between metastable states are governed by the Kramers escape rate $k = (ω_0ω_b/2π)\,e^{-ΔE/T}$. We make two contributions. First, we identify the EWC penalty term as an energy barrier whose height grows linearly with the number of accumulated tasks, yielding an exponential collapse of the transition rate predicted analytically and confirmed numerically. Second, we show that insight and repetitive learning correspond to two qualitatively distinct temperature protocols within the same Fokker--Planck equation: insight events produce transient spikes in $T(t)$ that drive rapid barrier crossing, whereas repetitive practice operates at a modestly elevated but fixed temperature, achieving transitions through sustained stochastic diffusion. These results establish a physically grounded framework for understanding plasticity and its failure in continual learning systems, and suggest principled design criteria for adaptive noise schedules in artificial intelligence.

### [163] [Semi-Markovian Dynamics of a Self-Propelled Particle in a Confined Environment: A Large-Deviation Study](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.04595)

Method: 采用半马尔可夫过程（semi-Markovian process）建模粒子在"正常运动相"（Phase 0）和"壁附着相"（Phase 1）之间的转变，分析两种不同场景：第一种包含老化逻辑的复位概率，第二种涉及两个活性相之间的交替。通过分析长时间极限下的标度累积生成函数（Scaled Cumulant Generating Function, SCGF）来研究动力学相变。

Result: 研究推导出粒子速度涨落中动力学相变（Dynamical Phase Transition, DPT）的条件，并证明系统根据老化强度（aging strength）的不同，会表现出不连续（一级）或连续（二级）的动力学相变。理论预测通过计算机模拟得到了验证。

Abstract: We study the large deviations of the time-integrated current for a self-propelled particle moving within a confined environment. The dynamics is modeled as a semi-Markovian process, where the transitions between a \textit{normal running phase} (Phase $0$) and a \textit{wall-attached phase} (Phase $1$) are governed by time-dependent reset probabilities. We study two different examples: In the first case, the particle undergoes a biased random walk in Phase $0$, while it intermittently resets and interacts with the container boundaries, remaining stationary in Phase $1$. In this scenario, the reset probabilities for transitions between the two phases follow an ``aging'' logic. In the second case, the particle alternates between two active phases: a Markovian Phase $0$ characterized by memoryless, downstream-biased motion, and a semi-Markovian Phase $1$ with a reversed, upstream bias representing boundary-attached navigation. Here, we assume a time-independent survival probability in Phase $0$ and a time-dependent one in Phase $1$. By analyzing the Scaled Cumulant Generating Function (SCGF) in the long-time limit, we derive the conditions for Dynamical Phase Transition (DPT)s in the fluctuations of the particle velocity. We demonstrate that, depending on the aging strength, the system exhibits either discontinuous (first-order) or continuous (second-order) DPTs. Analytical predictions are validated via computer simulations.

### [164] [Unified geometric formalism for dissipation and its fluctuations in finite-time microscopic heat engines](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.04620)
*Gentaro Watanabe,Guo-Hua Xu,Yuki Minami*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该论文开发了一个统一的几何框架，用于描述微观热机（microscopic heat engines）中平均耗散可用性（dissipated availability）及其涨落，在线性响应（linear-response）区域建立了基于平衡关联函数（equilibrium correlation functions）的度量张量（metric tensors）几何结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 微观热机在热力学量强烈涨落的区域运行，使得随机效应成为其性能的重要方面。然而，现有的有限时间热力学（finite-time thermodynamics）几何公式主要描述平均耗散，未能系统性地捕捉其涨落。

Method: 在线性响应区域，构建了由平衡关联函数构成的度量张量，为耗散及其涨落提供了共同的几何结构。该形式适用于包括马尔可夫跳跃过程（Markov jump processes）、过阻尼和欠阻尼布朗动力学（overdamped and underdamped Brownian dynamics）在内的随机系统。

Result: 该框架得出了平均耗散可用性及其方差的几何界限，从而也限制了效率及其涨落。建立了一个跨微观热机的统一几何描述，能够一致地描述平均耗散可用性及其涨落。

Conclusion: 该研究发展了一个统一的几何框架，系统地捕捉了微观热机中耗散的涨落，为有限时间热力学的几何描述提供了更全面的理论基础，适用于广泛的随机系统。

Abstract: Microscopic heat engines operate in regimes where thermodynamic quantities fluctuate strongly, making stochastic effects an essential aspect of their performance. However, existing geometric formulations of finite-time thermodynamics primarily characterize average dissipation and do not systematically capture its fluctuations. Here, we develop a unified geometric framework that consistently describes both the mean dissipated availability and its fluctuations. In the linear-response regime, we show that these quantities are governed by metric tensors constructed from equilibrium correlation functions, providing a common geometric structure for dissipation and its fluctuations. This framework yields geometric bounds on both the mean and variance of the dissipated availability, and thereby on the efficiency and its fluctuations. The formalism applies broadly to stochastic systems, including Markov jump processes and overdamped and underdamped Brownian dynamics, establishing a unified geometric description across microscopic heat engines.

</details>


### [165] [Cyclic Heat Engine with the Ising model: role of interactions and criticality](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.04730)
*Gustavo A. L. Forão,Arya Datta,Carlos E. Fiore,Andre C. Barato*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种基于伊辛模型（Ising model）的循环热机，通过同时调控温度和磁场实现热功转换。研究发现相互作用可以提升热机的功率和效率，并揭示了相变对热机性能的重要影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 热机作为经典热力学的基石，将热能转化为功，在微观热机、功率与效率权衡关系以及有限功率下卡诺效率可达性等方面仍是当代研究热点。研究者旨在探索基于伊辛模型的循环热机，以深入理解相互作用在热机中的作用机制。

Method: 研究提出了一种基于伊辛模型的循环热机，其热力学循环涉及温度和磁场的协同变化。分析了一维伊辛模型和平均场伊辛模型，这些模型允许获得简单的解析结果，为研究相互作用在循环热机中的作用提供了新视角。

Result: 研究发现相互作用可以同时增强热机的功率和效率。无相互作用时无法作为热机运行的系统，通过调节相互作用强度可以转变为热机。平均场模型揭示了相变对伊辛热机性能的重要性，由于自发磁化的出现，即使其中一个磁场设为零，平均场模型仍可作为热机运行。

Conclusion: 当功最大化时，最优参数在数值上与一个磁场为零且循环探索相变的机制一致。研究还分析了通过变化相互作用强度而保持温度低于临界温度的替代循环。虽然解析结果适用于大周期极限，但数值模拟显示功率随周期单调递减。

Abstract: Heat engines that convert thermal energy into work are a cornerstone of classical thermodynamics and remain an active area of contemporary research. Notable examples include microscopic heat engines, trade-off relations between power and efficiency, and the attainability of Carnot efficiency at finite power. We propose a cyclic heat engine based on the Ising model, in which the thermodynamic cycle involves variations of both temperature and magnetic field. We analyze the one-dimensional and mean-field Ising models, which allow for simple analytical results and provide new insight into the role of interactions in cyclic heat engines. In particular, we show that interactions can enhance both power and efficiency. Moreover, a system that does not operate as an engine in the absence of interactions can become an engine upon tuning the interaction strength. The mean-field model enables us to investigate the relevance of the phase transition for the performance of this Ising heat engine. Owing to the emergence of spontaneous magnetization, the mean-field model can still operate as an engine even when one of the magnetic fields is set to zero. Remarkably, when the work is maximized, we find that the optimal parameters are numerically consistent with this regime, in which one magnetic field vanishes and the cycle explores the phase transition. We also consider an alternative cycle for the mean-field model, obtained by varying the interaction strength while keeping both temperatures below the critical temperature and setting the magnetic field to zero throughout the cycle. The power and efficiency of this cycle are analyzed as well. Finally, while our analytical results are valid for the limit of large period we use numerical simulations for finite periods and show that the power decreases monotonically with the period.

</details>


### [166] [Analytical approach to subsystem resetting in generalized Kuramoto models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.04769)
*Rupak Majumder,Anish Acharya,Shamik Gupta*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文建立了分析库拉莫托型耦合振子系统（Kuramoto-type coupled-oscillator systems）中子系统重置（subsystem resetting）的通用理论框架，揭示了重置速率、重置子系统大小和重置配置如何影响稳态和相变，展示了子系统重置作为非平衡相互作用系统中集体动力学控制协议的潜力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究主要关注全局重置（global resetting），即所有自由度同时重置，而最近工作表明仅重置部分自由度（子系统重置）能显著改变相互作用多体系统的集体行为。本文旨在发展分析库拉莫托型耦合振子系统中子系统重置的通用理论框架。

Method: 基于连分数方法（continued-fraction approach），推导了非重置子系统稳态序参量（order parameter）的自洽方程，适用于含噪声和无噪声动力学以及具有任意相互作用谐波的模型。利用该框架系统研究了稳态和相变对重置速率、重置子系统大小和重置配置的依赖性。

Result: 子系统重置能够移动甚至抑制同步转变（synchronization transitions），并产生非平凡特征如重入行为（re-entrant behavior）和相边界重构（restructuring of phase boundaries）。在特定情况下（包括具有洛伦兹频率分布的无噪声库拉莫托模型），结果恢复了已知解析预测并将其推广到更一般设置。

Conclusion: 这些结果确立了子系统重置作为工程化非平衡相互作用系统中集体动力学的一种多功能控制协议（versatile control protocol），为调控复杂系统的同步行为提供了新途径。

Abstract: Stochastic resetting has emerged as a powerful mechanism for driving systems into nonequilibrium stationary states with tunable properties. While most existing studies focus on global resetting, where all degrees of freedom are simultaneously reset, recent work has shown that resetting only a subset of degrees of freedom (subsystem resetting) can qualitatively alter collective behavior in interacting many-body systems. In this work, we develop a general theoretical framework for analysing subsystem resetting in Kuramoto-type coupled-oscillator systems. Building on a continued-fraction approach, we derive self-consistent equations for the stationary-state order parameter of the non-reset subsystem, applicable to both noisy and noiseless dynamics and to models with arbitrary interaction harmonics. Using this framework, we systematically investigate how the stationary state and phase transitions depend on the resetting rate, the size of the reset subsystem, and the reset configuration. We show that subsystem resetting can shift or even suppress synchronization transitions, and can give rise to nontrivial features such as re-entrant behavior and restructuring of phase boundaries. In specific cases, including the noiseless Kuramoto model with a Lorentzian frequency distribution, our results recover known analytical predictions and extend them to more general settings. These results establish subsystem resetting as a versatile control protocol for engineering collective dynamics in nonequilibrium interacting systems.

</details>


### [167] [Boltzmann-Loschmidt dispute reloaded quantum 150 years later](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.04879)
*Leonardo Ermann,Alexei D. Chepelianskii,Dima L. Shepelyansky*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究通过解析和数值方法证明，在谐波势阱和脉冲光学晶格中的冷原子或离子的量子混沌扩散可以实现高达100%效率的时间反演，这与经典演化中指数级小误差破坏时间可逆性形成鲜明对比。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机源于1876年的玻尔兹曼-洛施密特争议（Boltzmann-Loschmidt dispute），该争议质疑了基于时间可逆经典运动方程的统计不可逆描述的可行性。本研究旨在从量子角度重新审视这一经典争议。

Method: 采用解析和数值方法研究冷原子或离子在谐波势阱（harmonic trap）和脉冲光学晶格（pulsed optical lattice）中的量子混沌扩散（quantum chaos diffusion）行为。通过分析该系统的动力学特性来探索时间反演的可能性。

Result: 研究发现量子混沌扩散可以实现高达100%效率的时间反演，这与经典演化形成鲜明对比——在经典系统中，指数级小误差会破坏时间可逆性。研究结果表明量子系统在时间反演方面具有独特的优势。

Conclusion: 现有实验技术能够从量子角度突显玻尔兹曼-洛施密特争议，量子系统中的时间反演效率远高于经典系统，这为理解统计不可逆性与时间可逆性之间的关系提供了新的量子视角。

Abstract: The Boltzmann-Loschmidt dispute of 1876 questioned the possibility of a statistical irreversible description by time reversible classical equations of motion of atoms. Here we show analytically and numerically that the quantum chaos diffusion of cold atoms, or ions, in a harmonic trap and pulsed optical lattice can be inverted back in time with up to 100\% efficiency. This is in sharp contrast to classical evolution where exponentially small errors break time reversibility. We argue that the existing experimental skills allow highlighting the Boltzmann-Loschmidt dispute from a quantum perspective.

</details>

### [168] [Totally nonnegative maximal tori and opposed Bruhat intervals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.03484)
*Grant T. Barkley,Steven N. Karp*

Main category: math.CO

TL;DR: 本文验证了Lusztig关于全正部分到全正极大环面空间映射满射性的猜想，研究了该空间的闭包，建立了与Bruhat区间对组合关系'对立性'的联系，并揭示了该空间可作为'通用旗幅面体'与理论物理中的幅面体相关联。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Lusztig (2024) 引入了代数群G的全正极大环面（totally positive maximal tori）空间𝒯_{>0}，并猜想从G的全正部分到该空间的映射是满射。本文旨在验证这一猜想，并研究𝒯_{>0}的闭包性质，同时建立与理论物理中幅面体（amplituhedron）的联系。

Method: 通过分析全非负Borel子群（totally nonnegative Borel subgroup）与全非正Borel子群的对立关系，将问题约化为Weyl群W的Bruhat区间对之间的新组合关系——"对立性"（opposition）。特别地，对G=SL_n（W为对称群）的情况提供了对立性的特征描述。

Result: 验证了Lusztig关于映射满射性的猜想，建立了闭包问题与Bruhat区间对立性组合关系的联系，并证伪了Lusztig (2021)关于全非负Borel子群的另一个猜想。同时证明了𝒯_{>0}可视为"通用旗幅面体"（universal flag amplituhedron），建立了与Arkani-Hamed和Trnka (2014)引入的幅面体的联系。

Conclusion: 本文完全解决了Lusztig关于全正极大环面空间映射满射性的猜想，建立了该空间闭包问题的组合刻画，并通过与幅面体的联系为研究𝒯_{>0}及其闭包提供了进一步的动机。这一工作连接了代数群理论、组合数学和理论物理中的相关概念。

Abstract: Lusztig (2024) recently introduced the space $\mathcal{T}_{>0}$ of totally positive maximal tori of an algebraic group $G$. Each such torus is the intersection of a totally positive Borel subgroup and a totally negative Borel subgroup. Lusztig defined a map from the totally positive part of $G$ to $\mathcal{T}_{>0}$ and conjectured that it is surjective. We verify this conjecture. We also examine the closure of $\mathcal{T}_{>0}$, by studying when a totally nonnegative Borel subgroup is opposed to a totally nonpositive Borel subgroup. Our main result reduces this problem to a new combinatorial relation between pairs of Bruhat intervals of the Weyl group $W$, which we call 'opposition'. We provide a characterization of opposition when $G = \text{SL}_n$ (and $W$ is the symmetric group). Along the way, we disprove another conjecture of Lusztig (2021) on totally nonnegative Borel subgroups. Finally, we connect $\mathcal{T}_{>0}$ to the amplituhedron introduced by Arkani-Hamed and Trnka (2014) in theoretical physics, by showing that $\mathcal{T}_{>0}$ can be regarded as a 'universal flag amplituhedron'. This gives further motivation for studying $\mathcal{T}_{>0}$ and its closure.

</details>

### [169] [Measurement of di-muons from 400 GeV/c protons interacting in a thick molybdenum/tungsten target](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.03661)
*The SHiP Collaboration*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: SHiP实验在CERN SPS上使用复刻靶标观测到J/ψ粒子产生，测量了包含衰变分支比的每核子产生截面，结果与NA50实验数据基本一致，未发现显著的靶内次级产生增强效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在通过SHiP实验的复刻靶标测量J/ψ粒子的产生截面，并与先前NA50实验的薄靶结果进行比较，以探究靶内次级产生效应（secondary production）对J/ψ产生的影响。

Method: 实验在CERN SPS上使用SHiP靶标的复刻版本，通过双μ子（di-muon）事件探测J/ψ产生。采用基于Pythia v8的蒙特卡洛模拟（Monte Carlo simulations）进行理论预测比较，并在中心质量系快度区间$0.3 < y_{cm} < 0.6$内测量产生截面。

Result: 测得包含J/ψ衰变到μ子分支比$B_{μμ}$的每核子产生截面为$(1.18~\pm~0.04~\pm~0.10)~\rm{nb}$/nucleon，与NA50外推结果$(0.99~\pm~0.04)~\rm{nb}$/nucleon基本一致。在系统误差范围内未观测到显著的靶内次级产生增强，级联碰撞（cascade collisions）贡献的上限为<32%。

Conclusion: SHiP实验的厚靶测量结果与NA50的薄靶外推值在误差范围内一致，表明靶内次级产生效应对J/ψ产生截面的影响不显著，为相关物理模型提供了重要实验约束。

Abstract: Di-muon events emanating from a replica of the SHiP target at the CERN SPS contain a clear signal of $J/ψ$~production. The production rate is in reasonable agreement with Monte Carlo simulations based on Pythia v8. For the interval in rapidity defined in the center of mass, $y_{cm}$, with the largest overlap with the NA50 measurement, $0.3 < y_{cm} < 0.6$, we obtain the production cross-section per nucleon $σ(J/ψ)/A$ including the branching ratios of $J/ψ$ decays into muons, $B_{μμ}$: $B_{μμ}σ(J/ψ)/A=(1.18~\pm~0.04~\pm~0.10)~\rm{nb}$/nucleon. This is to be compared to the NA50 extrapolated result (using a much thinner target): $B_{μμ}σ(J/ψ)/A=(0.99~\pm~0.04)~\rm{nb}$/nucleon. Within the systematic errors, no significant enhancement due to secondary production of $J/ψ$ inside the target is observed. An upper limit of possible contributions from cascade collisions of $<32\%$ is obtained.

</details>

Conclusion: 本研究展示了利用FCC-ee高亮度运行探测轻子门户暗物质的潜力。通过分析特定基准情景下的信号特征，研究为未来对撞机实验设定了对矢量样轻子质量和耦合强度的敏感性界限，为暗物质探测提供了重要的实验指导。

Abstract: This analysis delves into the lepton portal dark matter by utilizing Monte Carlo simulated samples from electron-positron collisions at the Future Circular Collider (FCC-ee), operating at a center of mass energy of 240 GeV and an integrated luminosity of 10.8 ab$^{-1}$. The study explores a specific benchmark scenario in which dark matter is represented as a scalar particle produced as a byproduct of a vector-like lepton. The key signal signature features missing transverse energy alongside dilepton events. Should new physics not be detected, this study establishes 95\% confidence level exclusion limits on the mass of the vector-like leptons and the Yukawa coupling.

### [172] [Geometry of the tt*-Toda equations I: universal centralizer and symplectic groupoids](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.04358)
*Martin A. Guest,Nan-Kuo Ho*

Main category: math.SG

TL;DR: 该论文研究了具有不规则奇点的亚纯连接（meromorphic connections）空间的几何结构，证明其构成一个（实）辛李群胚（symplectic Lie groupoid）。这些连接对应Cecotti-Vafa拓扑-反拓扑融合（tt*）方程的特定解，与超对称量子场论（supersymmetric quantum field theories）的形变相关。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机源于探索具有不规则奇点的亚纯连接空间的几何特性，这些连接在物理上对应Cecotti-Vafa拓扑-反拓扑融合（tt*）方程的特定解，与超对称量子场论的形变密切相关。

Method: 研究方法包括：首先证明李群（Lie group）的泛中心化子（universal centralizer）是Steinberg截面上的全纯辛群胚（holomorphic symplectic groupoid）；然后将分析限制在Toda型的tt*方程上，其单值数据（monodromy data）具有李理论描述。

Result: 主要结果表明：具有不规则奇点的特定亚纯连接空间构成一个（实）辛李群胚；该群胚结构源于对Toda型tt*方程的限制，其单值数据具有李理论描述。

Conclusion: 论文结论是：通过证明泛中心化子的群胚结构，建立了具有不规则奇点的亚纯连接空间与辛李群胚之间的几何联系，为理解tt*方程的解空间及其在超对称量子场论形变中的应用提供了新的几何框架。

Abstract: We investigate the geometry of a certain space of meromorphic connections with irregular singularities, and prove in particular that it is a (real) symplectic Lie groupoid. The connections have a physical meaning: they correspond to certain solutions of the topological-antitopological fusion (tt*) equations of Cecotti and Vafa, and hence to deformations of supersymmetric quantum field theories. The groupoid structure arises because we restrict ourselves to the tt* equations of Toda type, whose monodromy data has a Lie theoretic description. To obtain these results, we show first that the universal centralizer of a Lie group is a holomorphic symplectic groupoid over the Steinberg cross section.

</details>

### [173] [A pluricomplex error-function kernel at the edge of polynomial Bergman kernels](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.04661)
*L. D. Molag*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 该论文研究多项式Bergman核在指数变化权重下的局部行为，构建行列式点过程，证明在液滴边缘存在两种普适极限核：误差函数核及其多元推广，并在张量化和旋转对称两种设置下验证普适性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究多项式Bergman核在指数变化权重下的局部行为，特别是行列式点过程在液滴边缘的统计特性。旨在揭示随机矩阵理论中误差函数核的普适性在多元复分析中的推广。

Method: 使用多项式Bergman核构建$\mathbb C^d$上的行列式点过程，在势函数满足温和条件下分析点聚集在液滴边缘的行为。通过张量化分解和旋转对称两种不同设置验证普适性，并识别多元误差函数核在Bargmann-Fock空间中的再生子空间。

Result: 证明在液滴边缘附近，局部核行为由两种普适极限核描述：误差函数核及其多元推广。在张量化和旋转对称两种设置下验证普适性，识别多元误差函数核的再生子空间，并分析具有体简并性的正则边缘点行为。

Conclusion: 多项式Bergman核在指数权重下的边缘行为具有普适性，表现为误差函数核及其多元版本。该研究建立了随机矩阵理论与多元复分析之间的新联系，为行列式点过程的边缘统计提供了理论基础。

Abstract: We consider polynomial Bergman kernels with respect to exponentially varying weights $e^{-n \mathscr Q(z)}$ depending on a potential $\mathscr Q:\mathbb C^d\to\mathbb R$. We use these kernels to construct determinantal point processes on $\mathbb C^d$. Under mild conditions on the potential, the points are known to accumulate on a compact set $S_{\mathscr Q}$ called the droplet. We show that the local behavior of the kernel in the vicinity of the edge $\partial S_{\mathscr Q}$ is described in two different ways by universal limiting kernels. One of these limiting kernels is the error-function kernel, which is ubiquitous in random matrix theory, while the other limiting kernel is a new universal object: a multivariate version of the error-function kernel. We prove the universality in two qualitatively different settings: (i) the tensorized case where $\mathscr Q$ decomposes as a sum of planar potentials, and (ii) the case where $\mathscr Q$ is rotational symmetric. We also explicitly identify the subspace of the Bargmann-Fock space where the multivariate error-function kernel is reproducing. To treat regular edge points that exhibit a certain type of bulk degeneracy, we also find the behavior of the planar kernel with number of terms of order $o(n)$ instead of $n$. Lastly, we prove an edge scaling limit for counting statistics.

### [174] [Elephant random walk on the infinite dihedral group $\mathbb{Z}_2 * \mathbb{Z}_2$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.04922)
*Soumendu Sundar Mukherjee,Himasish Talukdar*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 本文研究无限二面体群（infinite dihedral group）$D_\infty \cong \mathbb{Z}_2 * \mathbb{Z}_2$上的大象随机游走（elephant random walk），发现其行为与$\mathbb{Z}$上的经典ERW不同：虽然符号位置的一阶和二阶行为与$\mathbb{Z}$上的简单对称随机游走一致，但记忆参数仅通过低阶修正项体现，不会产生超扩散（superdiffusion）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 先前研究发现在$d \ge 3$的正则树（regular trees）上，大象随机游走具有与简单随机游走相同的渐近速度。本文旨在探究$d=2$的特殊情况，特别是无限二面体群$D_\infty$上的ERW行为，以理解局部代数关系对记忆效应的影响。

Method: 研究无限二面体群$D_\infty \cong \mathbb{Z}_2 * \mathbb{Z}_2$上的大象随机游走，该游走是非马尔可夫（non-Markovian）过程。通过分析游走者的符号位置（signed location），并与$\mathbb{Z}$上的简单对称随机游走（simple symmetric random walk）进行比较。

Result: $D_\infty$上ERW的符号位置的一阶和二阶行为与$\mathbb{Z}$上的简单对称随机游走一致。记忆参数仅通过低阶修正项体现，该修正项可表示为$\mathbb{Z}$上大象随机游走的显式泛函（explicit functional）。与$\mathbb{Z}$上观察到的超扩散不同，$D_\infty$上的ERW不会出现超扩散行为。

Conclusion: 大象随机游走对局部代数关系敏感：尽管$D_\infty$是虚拟阿贝尔群（virtually abelian）且包含$\mathbb{Z}$作为有限指数子群，但其生成元（generators）的对合性质（involutive nature）有效地中和了记忆效应，排除了任何潜在的超扩散行为。

Abstract: Elephant random walks were studied recently in \cite{mukherjee2025elephant} on the groups $\mathbb{Z}^{*d_1} * \mathbb{Z}_2^{*d_2}$ whose Cayley graphs are infinite $d$-regular trees with $d = 2d_1 + d_2$. It was found that for $d \ge 3$, the elephant walk is ballistic with the same asymptotic speed $\frac{d - 2}{d}$ as the simple random walk and the memory parameter appears only in the rate of convergence to the limiting speed. In the $d = 2$ case, there are two such groups, both having the bi-infinite path as their Cayley graph. For $(d_1, d_2) = (1, 0)$, the walk is the usual elephant random walk on $\mathbb{Z}$, which exhibits anomalous diffusion. In this article, we study the other case, namely $(d_1, d_2) = (0, 2)$, which corresponds to the infinite dihedral group $D_\infty \cong \mathbb{Z}_2 * \mathbb{Z}_2$. Unlike the classical ERW on $\mathbb{Z}$, which is a time-inhomogeneous Markov chain, the ERW on $D_{\infty}$ is non-Markovian. We show that the first and second order behaviours of the \emph{signed location} of the walker agree with those of the simple symmetric random walk on $\mathbb{Z}$, with the memory parameter essentially manifesting itself via a lower order correction term that can be written as an explicit functional of the elephant walk on $\mathbb{Z}$. Our result demonstrates that unlike the simple random walk, the elephant walk is sensitive to local algebraic relations. Indeed, although $D_{\infty}$ is virtually abelian, containing $\mathbb{Z}$ as a finite-index subgroup, the involutive nature of its generators effectively neutralises memory, thereby ruling out any potential superdiffusive behaviour, in contrast to the superdiffusion observed on its abelian cousin $\mathbb{Z}$.

</details>

### [175] [On the instability of some upward propagating, exact, nonlinear mountain waves](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.03620)
*Christian Puntini*

Main category: physics.ao-ph

TL;DR: 使用短波长不稳定性方法，研究向上传播的山地波精确解在干绝热流假设下的线性不稳定性，发现当波陡度超过临界阈值1/3时流动变得不稳定。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究由Constantin (2023)推导的向上传播山地波精确解的线性不稳定性，该解基于干绝热流（dry adiabatic flow）假设。旨在理解此类大气波动的稳定性条件及其对三维流体运动的影响。

Method: 采用短波长不稳定性方法（short-wavelength instability method），将稳定性问题简化为沿流体轨迹的常微分方程组分析。基于拉格朗日坐标（Lagrangian coordinates）下的解表示进行不稳定性分析。

Result: 当波陡度（wave steepness）超过临界阈值1/3时，流动变得不稳定。分析显示在对流层顶（tropopause）下方几百米处存在不稳定层，最终可能导致混沌的三维流体运动（chaotic 3-dimensional fluid motion）。

Conclusion: 向上传播的山地波在波陡度超过1/3时会发生线性不稳定性，特别是在对流层顶下方形成不稳定层，这为理解大气中波破碎和湍流生成机制提供了理论依据。

Abstract: Using the short-wavelength instability method, we investigate the linear instability of an exact solution describing upward-propagating mountain waves, derived in A. Constantin, \emph{J. Phys. A: Math. Theor.} (2023), under the assumption of a dry adiabatic flow. Within this approach, the stability problem reduces to analysing a system of ordinary differential equations along fluid trajectories. Our results show that the flow becomes unstable when the wave steepness exceeds the critical threshold of $\frac{1}{3}$. Given the representation of the solution in Lagrangian coordinates, the instability analysis will show the existence of an unstable layer of few hundred meters beneath the tropopause where instability may occur, finally leading to a chaotic 3-dimensional fluid motion.

### [176] [A Pontryagin class obstruction for purely electric and purely magnetic Weyl curvature tensors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.03707)
*Thijs de Kok*

Main category: math.DG

TL;DR: 该论文研究了4k维伪黎曼流形上是否存在纯电性（PE）或纯磁性（PM）的黎曼或外尔曲率张量，通过庞特里亚金形式（Pontryagin forms）的乘积在最高阶外幂中的消失性，推导出这类度量的上同调障碍（cohomological obstructions）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探讨所有允许洛伦兹度量的流形是否也允许具有纯电性（purely electric, PE）或纯磁性（purely magnetic, PM）外尔曲率张量（Weyl curvature tensor）的度量。这一问题与爱因斯坦方程（Einstein equations）精确解的分类相关，特别是与几种佩特罗夫子型（Petrov subtypes）的洛伦兹度量的存在性有关。

Method: 方法基于证明在4k维标量积空间上，所有在方向反转等距映射作用下为偶或奇的代数曲率张量（algebraic curvature tensors），其庞特里亚金形式（Pontryagin forms）的乘积在最高阶外幂中消失。利用这一结果推导出具有PE或PM黎曼或外尔曲率张量的4k维伪黎曼流形上，所有庞特里亚金类（Pontryagin classes）乘积在最高阶德拉姆上同调（de Rham cohomology）中的消失性。

Result: 对于紧致流形，该研究得出了非平凡的上同调障碍（cohomological obstructions），阻碍了具有全局PE或PM黎曼或外尔曲率张量的伪黎曼度量的存在。这些障碍可应用于由非退化脐点超曲面（nondegenerate umbilic hypersurfaces）构成的叶状结构，这些超曲面可能作为时空的时间切片出现。

Conclusion: 研究结论表明，通过庞特里亚金形式乘积的消失性，可以推导出具有PE或PM曲率张量的伪黎曼度量的上同调障碍。这些障碍不仅与佩特罗夫子型的洛伦兹度量存在性相关，还可应用于时空几何中的叶状结构分析。

Abstract: Do all manifolds that admit Lorentzian metrics also admit such metrics that have a purely electric (PE) or purely magnetic (PM) Weyl curvature tensor? To (partially) answer this question, we show that for all algebraic curvature tensors on a $4k$-dimensional scalar product space that are even or odd under the action of a orientation-reversing isometry, the products of Pontryagin forms that land in the top-degree exterior power of the dual vector space vanish. We use this to derive the vanishing of all products of Pontryagin classes that land in the top-degree de Rham cohomology of a $4k$-dimensional pseudo-Riemannian manifold with a PE or PM Riemann or Weyl curvature tensor. For compact manifolds, this gives nontrivial cohomological obstructions to the existence of such pseudo-Riemannian metrics with globally PE or PM Riemann or Weyl curvature tensors. These obstructions can be linked to the existence of Lorentzian metrics of several Petrov subtypes, which play an important role in classifying exact solutions to the Einstein equations. Moreover, they can be applied to foliations by nondegenerate umbilic hypersurfaces, which may appear as timeslices of spacetimes.

</details>

### [177] [Constructing a Quantum Twisting Microscope: Design Insights and Experimental Considerations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.03483)
*Sayanwita Biswas,Ranjani Ramachandran,Patrick Irvin,Jeremy Levy*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该论文详细介绍了量子扭转显微镜（Quantum Twisting Microscope, QTM）的构建与测试细节，这是一种能够测量层状材料中扭转角（twist angle）依赖电子特性的扫描探针仪器。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 开发量子扭转显微镜旨在实现对层状材料中扭转角依赖电子特性的精确测量，为研究范德华材料（van der Waals materials）、复杂氧化物异质结构和手性系统中的扭转角相关现象提供实验工具。

Method: 基于商用原子力显微镜（atomic force microscope, AFM）的开放几何结构，集成了旋转和平移平台；采用聚焦离子束沉积（focused ion beam deposition）制备探针和石墨转移技术，开发了具有集成旋转功能的自定义平台组装和多步对准程序。

Result: 通过对石墨层间电导（conductance）随扭转角变化的测量，观察到清晰的60度周期性，这与六方晶格对称性一致；在21.8度和38.2度等可公度扭转角（commensurate twist angles）附近观察到电导增强，证实了仪器解析晶体学扭转角依赖输运特征的能力。

Conclusion: 量子扭转显微镜的成功构建和验证使其成为研究扭转角相关现象的有效工具；通过提供详细的构建和操作指南，旨在使具有标准AFM基础设施的研究组能够使用QTM技术，促进相关领域的研究发展。

Abstract: We report the details of construction and testing of a Quantum Twisting Microscope, a recently developed scanning probe instrument that enables twist angle dependent electronic measurements on layered materials. Our implementation is based on a commercial atomic force microscope whose open geometry beneath the scan head allows integration of the rotation and translation stages required for QTM operation. We describe the complete fabrication process including tip preparation by focused ion beam deposition and graphite transfer, custom stage assembly with integrated rotation capability, and multistep alignment procedures. To validate the instrument, we perform conductance measurements between graphite layers as a function of twist angle, observing clear 60 degree periodicity consistent with the hexagonal lattice symmetry and conductance enhancements near the commensurate twist angles of 21.8 and 38.2 degrees. These results confirm the instruments ability to resolve crystallographic twist angle dependent transport features. By providing detailed construction and operational guidelines, we aim to make QTM technology accessible to research groups with standard AFM infrastructure, enabling investigations of twist angle dependent phenomena in van der Waals materials, complex oxide heterostructures and chiral systems.

</details>


### [178] [An argument why the Spinterface model cannot explain the chirality induced spin selectivity effect](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.03719)
*J. Fransson*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究分析表明，在金属-手性分子界面，金属的强自旋轨道耦合不足以稳定形成局域自旋矩，且电子通量（无论是否自旋极化）也无法促成自旋矩的形成。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 针对手性诱导自旋选择性效应中，手性分子吸附于金属表面可能促进界面局域自旋矩形成的观点，研究旨在通过理论分析检验这一机制的有效性。

Method: 采用一般性论证和有效建模方法，对金属-手性分子界面的相关物理构型进行理论分析，特别关注强自旋轨道耦合的作用机制。

Result: 分析表明，金属中的强自旋轨道耦合并非形成稳定界面自旋矩的充分机制；同时，无论电子通量是否自旋极化，都无法为自旋矩形成提供必要条件。

Conclusion: 金属强自旋轨道耦合不能有效维持界面稳定自旋矩，电子通量亦无法促成自旋矩形成，这对理解手性诱导自旋选择性效应的微观机制具有重要意义。

Abstract: In the context of chirality induced spin selectivity effect, it has been argued that a chiral molecule when adsorbed on a metal facilitates the formation of a local spin moment at the interface between the metal and molecule, given a strong spin-orbit coupling in the metal. The possibility for such spin moment formation is analyzed in terms of general arguments and effective modeling of a pertinent set-up. The conclusion from this analysis is that a strong spin-orbit coupling in the metal does not provide a sufficient mechanism to sustain a stabilized spin moment at the interface. It is, moreover, shown that an electron flux in to or out from the molecule does not provide conditions for a spin moment formation, regardless of whether the flux is spin-polarized or not.

### [179] [Quantum exciton solid with embedded electron-hole solids in double-layer WSe2](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.03740)
*Meizhen Huang,Zefei Wu,Chenxuan Lou,S. T. Chui,Ning Wang*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究在双层WSe₂/六方氮化硼异质结中，通过调控电子和空穴密度，观测到库仑拖拽电阻（Coulomb drag resistance）出现量子化平台，揭示了激子固体（exciton solid）及其量子边缘缺陷的输运机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在探索双层过渡金属硫化物异质结中，电子-空穴密度调控下形成的极端量子固体态（extreme quantum solid states），特别是激子固体及其量子缺陷态的强关联输运现象。

Method: 采用双层WSe₂堆叠在六方氮化硼薄层两侧的异质结构，通过调控不同电子和空穴密度进行输运测量。在Corbino几何结构中进行了无边缘输运实验，并进行了声子计算（phonon calculations）验证固体态的稳定性。

Result: 当电子与空穴数量相等时形成激子固体，其量子边缘缺陷输运产生库仑拖拽电阻平台（约$-h/(4e^2)$）。当电子密度超过空穴时，过剩电子形成嵌入固体，阻塞一个输运通道，产生第二个平台（约$-h/(2e^2)$）。Corbino几何中平台消失，出现三个电阻峰，对应激子固体和两类空穴固体。

Conclusion: 研究建立了极端量子固体态的新类别，揭示了激子固体中量子边缘空位-间隙对（quantum edge vacancy-interstitial pairs）的一维输运机制，为研究涉及量子缺陷态的强关联量子输运现象开辟了新途径。

Abstract: We studied double-layer WSe2 stacked on opposite sides of thin layers of hexagonal Boron nitride with different densities of electrons and holes. For a fixed hole density, the Coulomb drag resistance is found to exhibit plateaus approximately equal to $-h/(4e^2)$ and $-h/(2e^2)$ as the electron density is changed. When the number of electrons is equal to the number of holes, an exciton solid forms whose transport of quantum edge defects gives rise to the drag resistance. When the electron and hole densities are different, the excess electrons form a solid embedded in the exciton solid. The Coulomb drag resistance of the exciton solid comes from the one-dimensional transport of the two lowest energy channels of quantum edge vacancy-interstitial pairs. This corresponds to the first plateau. With the embedded solid, one of these channels is blocked. This corresponds to the second plateau. Transport experiments in the Corbino geometry with no edges and extra heavier holes were carried out. The plateaus disappeared. Three peaks in the resistance at different hole densities were observed. We interpret that the three peaks correspond to the commensurate exciton and two classes of hole solids. We performed phonon calculations of these states and found that the stability of these exciton-based quantum solids shows good agreement with experiment. Our results establish classes of extreme quantum solid states, opening additional avenues for the study of strongly correlated quantum transport phenomena involving quantum defect states.

</details>


### [180] [Theoretical study of spin-dependent transport in WSe$_2$-based vertical spin valves](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.03762)
*Yibo Wang,Yuchen Liu,Xinhe Wang,Wang Yang*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该论文理论研究了基于过渡金属硫族化合物（TMD）的垂直自旋阀中的自旋依赖输运，以WSe₂为例，揭示了磁阻随WSe₂厚度的振荡依赖关系，并识别出类似法布里-珀罗干涉的贡献可导致负磁阻。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在从理论上理解WSe₂基自旋阀中观察到的负磁阻现象，并为可调谐自旋电子器件的设计提供见解。

Method: 采用异质结的有效哈密顿量（effective Hamiltonians）和朗道尔公式（Landauer formula），在转移矩阵方法（transfer-matrix approach）框架内推导透射和反射系数。

Result: 计算显示磁阻随WSe₂厚度呈现振荡依赖关系，尤其在费米能级（Fermi level）调至价带最大值附近时；类似法布里-珀罗（Fabry-Pérot-like）干涉贡献可增强甚至在某些厚度区间诱导负磁阻。

Conclusion: 研究结果为WSe₂基自旋阀中观察到的负磁阻提供了定性理解，并为可调谐自旋电子器件的设计提供了有用见解。

Abstract: We theoretically investigate spin-dependent transport in a TMD-based vertical spin valve, taking WSe$_2$ as a representative example. Using effective Hamiltonians for the heterostructure and the Landauer formula, we derive the transmission and reflection coefficients within a transfer-matrix approach. The calculated magnetoresistance shows an oscillatory dependence on the WSe$_2$ thickness when the Fermi level is tuned near the valence-band maximum. The effects of gate voltage and exchange fields on the magnetoresistance are further analyzed. We also identify a Fabry-Pérot-like interference contribution to the magnetoresistance, which can enhance or even induce negative magnetoresistance in certain thickness regimes. Our results provide a qualitative understanding of the negative magnetoresistance observed in WSe$_2$-based spin valves and may offer useful insights for the design of tunable spintronic devices.

</details>


### [181] [Nonreciprocal current induced by dissipation in time-reversal symmetric systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.04520)
*Takahiro Anan,Sota Kitamura,Takahiro Morimoto*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了时间反演对称性下非中心对称晶体中的非互易电流响应（nonreciprocal current response），揭示了这种电流通过带间过程在耗散系统中产生，并与称为位移矢量（shift vector）的几何量密切相关。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在理解非中心对称晶体在时间反演对称性条件下的非互易电流响应机制，特别关注耗散系统中通过带间过程产生的电流现象。

Method: 采用理论分析展示非互易电流通过带间过程在耗散系统中出现，并建立电流与位移矢量（shift vector）的数学关系。通过一维Rice-Mele模型进行数值模拟验证理论预测。

Result: 研究发现非互易电流与寿命τ成反比，且与位移矢量这一几何量密切相关。该电流机制特别适用于能隙（energy gap）与弛豫强度（relaxation strength）相当的小能隙系统（minigap systems）。

Conclusion: 研究揭示了非互易电流在耗散系统中的产生机制，建立了电流响应与几何量位移矢量的理论联系，为一维Rice-Mele模型中的非互易电流现象提供了数值验证。

Abstract: We study nonreciprocal current response in noncentrosymmetric crystals under time-reversal symmetry. We show that the nonreciprocal current appears in a dissipative system through interband processes. The nonreciprocal current is inversely proportional to the lifetime $τ$ and has a close relationship to the geometric quantity called the shift vector. The current mechanism is suitable for minigap systems where the energy gap and relaxation strength are comparable. We present a numerical simulation of the nonreciprocal current in the one-dimensional Rice--Mele model.

</details>

### [182] [Poisson Vertex Algebra of Seiberg-Witten Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.03500)
*Ahsan Z. Khan*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文研究了四维$\mathcal{N}=2$纯$SU(2)$规范理论中全纯-拓扑超荷$Q$-上同调局部算符空间的泊松顶点代数结构，提出了一个明确的泊松顶点代数$A$作为微扰理论所有阶的候选代数，并探讨了其与非微扰修正的关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究四维$\mathcal{N}=2$规范理论中全纯-拓扑超荷（holomorphic-topological supercharge）$Q$-上同调局部算符空间的代数结构，特别是纯$SU(2)$规范理论的泊松顶点代数（Poisson vertex algebra）性质。

Method: 提出一个明确的泊松顶点代数$A$，声称其在微扰理论所有阶与全纯-拓扑可观测量代数同构；计算$A$的希尔伯特-庞加莱级数（Hilbert-Poincaré series）；引入进一步微分$Q_{\text{inst}}$来捕捉非微扰修正。

Result: $A$的希尔伯特-庞加莱级数精化了纯$SU(2)$理论的舒尔指数（Schur index）；$A$允许进一步微分$Q_{\text{inst}}$，其计算了该微分的上同调，提出了塞伯格-维腾理论（Seiberg-Witten theory）非微扰全纯-拓扑可观测量的明确候选空间。

Conclusion: 该研究为四维$\mathcal{N}=2$纯$SU(2)$规范理论的全纯-拓扑可观测量代数提供了明确的泊松顶点代数描述，并提出了包含非微扰修正的候选代数结构，深化了对塞伯格-维腾理论代数结构的理解。

Abstract: The space of local operators in the $Q$-cohomology of the holomorphic-topological supercharge in a four-dimensional $\mathcal{N}=2$ theory carries the structure of a Poisson vertex algebra. This note studies the Poisson vertex algebra associated to the pure $\mathcal{N}=2$ gauge theory with gauge group $SU(2)$. We propose an explicit Poisson vertex algebra $A$, claimed to be isomorphic to the algebra of holomorphic-topological observables to all orders in perturbation theory. We compute the Hilbert-Poincaré series of $A$ and show that it refines the Schur index of the pure $SU(2)$ theory. We show that $A$ admits a further differential $Q_{\text{inst}}$ which we hypothesize captures non-perturbative corrections, and compute the cohomology of this differential. We thus present an explicit candidate for the space of non-perturbative holomorphic-topological observables of Seiberg-Witten theory.

</details>


### [183] [How to Expose a Black Hole](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.03720)
*Ashoke Sen*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种机制，通过让黑洞在时空背景中移动至弱耦合区域，使其平滑过渡为无事件视界的正常量子态，从而避免信息悖论问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 基于Horowitz和Polchinski的对应原理（correspondence principle），当弦耦合（string coupling）足够小时，弦理论中的许多黑洞可连续形变为涉及D-膜（D-branes）和基本弦（fundamental strings）的常规量子系统。因此，研究黑洞在时空背景中移动并转化为无事件视界的量子态，为解决黑洞信息悖论提供了可能途径。

Method: 通过考虑时空中的一种构型，其中伸缩子（dilaton）在适当范围内变化，使黑洞在此背景中移动。关键在于选择合适的背景参数：伸缩子变化既不能太快（以免破坏绝热近似或导致时空本身坍缩成黑洞），也不能太慢（以免黑洞移动所需时间超过其蒸发时间）。

Result: 研究表明，通过适当选择背景参数，可以避免上述障碍。黑洞向弱耦合区域（weak coupling region）的温和运动能够将其转化为无事件视界的正常量子态，其微观态不再隐藏在事件视界之后。

Conclusion: 该机制表明，通过精心设计的时空背景，黑洞可以平滑过渡为常规量子系统，从而为黑洞信息问题提供了一种潜在的解决方案。这避免了信息悖论中关于微观态是否永久隐藏在事件视界之后的困境。

Abstract: According to the correspondence principle of Horowitz and Polchinski, many black holes in string theory are continuously deformed to usual quantum systems involving D-branes and fundamental strings when the string coupling becomes sufficiently small. Therefore if we consider a configuration in space-time where the dilaton varies over an appropriate range, then a black hole moving in such a background will smoothly transition from the black hole state to a normal quantum state whose microstates are not hidden behind an event horizon. The possible obstruction to this mechanism comes from the fact that if the dilaton varies too fast then the adiabatic approximation may break down and / or the ambient space-time itself may collapse to a black hole and get hidden from the asymptotic observer. On the other hand, if the dilaton varies too slowly then the time that it takes for the black hole to travel the required distance will exceed the evaporation time of the black hole. We show that by choosing the background appropriately these obstructions can be avoided and a gentle motion towards the weak coupling region will convert the black hole into a normal quantum state without an event horizon.

</details>


### [184] [Causality, the Kovtun-Son-Starinets bound, and a novel sum rule for spectral densities](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.04222)
*G. Yu. Prokhorov,O. V. Teryaev*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文直接证明了有限距离处Unruh辐射的剪切黏度与熵密度之比具有普适性，满足η/s = 1/(4πc_s²)关系，建立了Kovtun-Son-Starinets边界与因果性的紧密联系，并提出了新的求和规则。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究Unruh辐射的输运性质，旨在建立著名的Kovtun-Son-Starinets边界与因果性之间的直接联系，并为极端加速介质（如相对论重离子碰撞中产生的夸克-胶子等离子体）中的耗散输运现象提供新视角。

Method: 直接计算有限距离处Unruh辐射的局部剪切黏度与熵密度之比，分析其与声速c_s的关系；通过Rindler空间中热辐射的各向同性条件推导新的求和规则，并在共形场论和自由大质量Dirac场中验证其有效性。

Result: 发现η/s = 1/(4πc_s²)的普适关系，由于c_s² ≤ 1的因果性限制，建立了与Kovtun-Son-Starinets边界的直接联系；体黏度与剪切黏度之比饱和了全息方法预测的另一个边界；提出的新求和规则在共形场论和自由大质量Dirac场中得到验证。

Conclusion: Unruh辐射的黏度-熵密度比具有普适性并受因果性约束，新提出的求和规则验证了Pascal定律，为极端加速介质中的耗散输运现象提供了新的理论框架，与相对论重离子碰撞中的夸克-胶子等离子体研究相关。

Abstract: We directly show that the local ratio of the shear viscosity to the entropy density for Unruh radiation at a finite distance from the horizon is universal and satisfies the relation $ η/s = 1/(4πc_s^2) $, which involves the speed of sound $ c_s $. Since $ c_s^2 \leq 1 $ by causality, this establishes the close connection between the famous Kovtun-Son-Starinets bound and causality. Moreover, we show that the ratio of bulk to shear viscosity saturates another well-known bound for the bulk viscosity, predicted within holographic approach. We also show that the condition of isotropy of thermal radiation in the Rindler space leads to a novel sum rule relating the $ c^{(0)}(μ) $ and $ c^{(2)}(μ) $ spectral densities, and we explicitly demonstrate its validity for conformal field theory and free massive Dirac fields in any number of dimensions. The sum rule provides the validity of Pascal law and bears some similarity with Burkhardt-Cottingham sum rule for spin-dependent parton distributions. Our result suggests a new perspective on dissipative transport phenomena in media undergoing extreme acceleration, such as quark-gluon plasma created in relativistic heavy-ion collisions.

</details>


### [185] [Superradiant Suppression of Non-minimally Coupled Scalar fields for a Rotating Charged dS Black Hole in Conformal Weyl Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.04352)
*Owen Gartlan,Jacob March,Leo Rodriguez,Shanshan Rodriguez,Yihan Shen*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文解析研究了旋转带电de Sitter黑洞时空中，大质量带电共形耦合标量场的超辐射散射现象，对比了广义相对论（GR）和四阶共形（Weyl平方）引力（CWG）理论。研究发现CWG理论中的超辐射放大效应相对于GR理论受到抑制，特别是在大质量场情况下，宇宙学区域存在指数级强抑制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在分析旋转带电de Sitter黑洞时空中，大质量带电共形耦合标量场的超辐射散射现象。研究动机在于比较两种引力理论——广义相对论（General Relativity, GR）和四阶共形（Weyl平方）引力（Conformal Weyl-squared Gravity, CWG）——对超辐射放大效应的影响差异。

Method: 对于无质量带电共形耦合标量场，利用新发现的Heun方程与二维共形场论中Belavin-Polyakov-Zamolodchikov（BPZ）方程半经典极限之间的对应关系，以小参数标度展开求解超辐射放大因子。对于大质量带电共形耦合标量场，采用WKB方法推导放大因子的数量级近似，分别处理宇宙学区域和$r_+\ll r \ll r_c$区域（其中$r_+$和$r_c$分别为外视界和宇宙学视界）。

Result: 在研究的参数范围内，观察到CWG理论中的超辐射放大效应相对于GR理论受到抑制。特别是在大质量场情况下，宇宙学区域存在指数级强抑制，抑制程度约为$e^{-2μΛ^{-1/2}}$量级，其中μ为质量参数，Λ为宇宙学常数。

Conclusion: 研究表明，在旋转带电de Sitter黑洞时空中，四阶共形引力理论（CWG）相对于广义相对论（GR）会抑制带电共形耦合标量场的超辐射放大效应。这一抑制效应在大质量场情况下尤为显著，表现为宇宙学区域的指数级强抑制，揭示了不同引力理论对黑洞超辐射现象的重要差异。

Abstract: In this study, we present an analytical investigation of the superradiant scattering of a massive charged conformally coupled scalar field in rotating charged $de~Sitter$ black hole spacetimes within two gravitational theories: General Relativity (GR) and fourth-order Conformal (Weyl-squared) Gravity (CWG). For the massless charged conformally coupled scalar, we exploit a recently discovered correspondence between the Heun equation and the semiclassical limit of Belavin-Polyakov-Zamolodchikov (BPZ) equations in two-dimensional conformal field theory to solve for the superradiant amplification factors as controlled expansions in a small parameter scaling. For the massive charged conformally coupled scalar, we use WKB methods to derive an order of magnitude approximation for the amplification factors in the cosmological region in terms of those in the region $r_+\ll r \ll r_c$ where $r_+$ and $r_c$ are the outer and cosmological event horizons, respectively. For both the massless and massive sectors, suppression of superradiant amplification in CWG relative to that in GR is observed across the parameter regimes studied. Particularly, in the massive sector, we find strong exponential suppression of superradiant amplification on the order of $e^{-2μΛ^{-1/2}}$ in the cosmological region.

</details>


### [186] [Anomalies in family unification models from bordism classification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.04393)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用可逆场论的配边分类框架，重点研究以例外群E7及其子群构建的目标空间模型。通过Atiyah-Hirzebruch谱序列显式计算相关配边群，分析编码在配边群挠部分中的全局σ模型反常。

Result: 证明了全局σ模型反常的缺失，这些反常编码在相关配边群的挠部分中。在构建家族统一模型时，识别了相关配边群，并证明了当陪集空间的各向同性子群被规范化时不会出现全局反常。

Conclusion: 基于可逆场论的配边分类方法，成功分析了家族统一模型中的反常问题，证明了在特定条件下（当陪集空间的各向同性子群被规范化时）不会出现全局反常，为这类模型的构建提供了理论一致性保证。

Abstract: We study anomalies in family unification models within the framework of the bordism classification of invertible field theories. These models are based on four-dimensional $\mathcal{N}=1$ supersymmetric nonlinear sigma models, in which the three generations of quarks and leptons arise as superpartners of the sigma model fields. We focus on models whose target spaces are constructed from the exceptional group $E_{7}$ and its subgroups. For the consistency of the theory, sigma model anomalies must be cancelled. We show the absence of global sigma model anomalies, which are encoded in the torsion part of the relevant bordism groups, by explicitly computing these groups using the Atiyah-Hirzebruch spectral sequence. In constructing family unification models, symmetries acting on the coset spaces are gauged, which may introduce additional anomalies. We identify the relevant bordism groups in this setting and demonstrate that no global anomalies arise when the isotropy subgroup of the coset space is gauged.

### [188] [The Gauge-Invariant Mass Function](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.04569)
*Kang-Sin Choi*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文提出在规范理论（gauge theories）中，重整化（renormalization）能够定义出与规范无关（gauge-invariant）的质量函数和顶点函数，从而为虚粒子（virtual particle）提供与壳上粒子（on-shell particle）同样明确的定义。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在规范理论中，场质量（mass of a field）传统上被视为纯粹的壳上概念（on-shell concept）：极点质量（pole mass）是规范不变的，但壳外传播子（off-shell propagator）缺乏规范不变的质量定义。这限制了虚粒子的理论描述。

Method: 作者通过重整化方法，在任意虚度（virtuality）下定义出规范不变的质量函数（gauge-invariant mass function）和规范不变的顶点函数（gauge-invariant vertex）。该方法将重整化群（renormalization group）技术应用于规范理论的非壳外（off-shell）区域。

Result: 研究结果表明，虚粒子获得了与壳上粒子同样明确的定义，其区别不再是动力学（dynamical）的，而纯粹是运动学（kinematic）的。这为规范理论中非壳外物理量的描述提供了新的理论基础。

Conclusion: 重整化能够为规范理论中的虚粒子定义出规范不变的质量函数和顶点函数，从而统一了壳上和壳外粒子的理论描述框架，消除了传统上对质量概念的局限性理解。

Abstract: In gauge theories, the mass of a field has been regarded as a purely on-shell concept: the pole mass is gauge-invariant, but the off-shell propagator has had no gauge-invariant definition of mass. We show that renormalization defines a gauge-invariant mass function at every virtuality, together with a gauge-invariant vertex. The virtual particle becomes as well defined as the on-shell one: the distinction is not dynamical but purely kinematic.

</details>


### [189] [New Solutions for RG Equations in QCD](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.04766)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究者构造了重整化群方程在渐近区域（asymptotic regime）的简单解析解，这些解具有显式形式并能自动求和微扰理论（perturbative theory）各阶中的领头对数（leading logarithms）、次领头对数（subleading logarithms）等项。

Result: 所得解析解能轻松重现逆对数展开（inverse logarithm expansion），并为进一步的求和及渐近行为（asymptotic behaviour）的改进提供了便利。

Conclusion: 该研究成功构建了QCD重整化群方程的简单解析解，这些解不仅具有显式形式，还能系统求和所有阶的对数项，为渐近行为的分析和改进提供了有效工具。

Abstract: We construct simple analytical solutions of renormalization group equations for the running coupling and for the Green functions in QCD in the asymptotic regime. These solutions have an explicit form and subsequently sum up the leading, subleading, and so on logarithms in all orders of PT. They easily reproduce the inverse logarithm expansion and allow for further summation and improvement of the asymptotic behaviour.

### [190] [Exponentially Long Evaporation of Noncommutative Black Hole](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.04774)
*Pei-Ming Ho,Wei-Hsiang Shao,Takuya Yoda*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了非对易时空（noncommutative spacetime）中的霍金辐射（Hawking radiation），发现时空非对易性会改变辐射场与背景几何的相互作用，导致辐射在"扰乱时间（scrambling time）"后显著衰减，从而使黑洞蒸发时间呈指数级延长。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探讨非对易时空框架下霍金辐射的性质，特别是检验传统霍金辐射鲁棒性论证在非对易时空中的有效性，因为非对易时空固有的非局域性（nonlocality）可能改变辐射过程。

Method: 研究方法基于分析由物质壳层坍缩形成的动态黑洞，考察非对易时空如何修正辐射场与背景几何的相互作用，其中坍缩壳层会因出射霍金模式的动量而发生有效偏移。

Result: 研究结果表明，非对易时空中的霍金辐射在扰乱时间后显著衰减，导致黑洞蒸发时间呈指数级延长，这挑战了传统霍金辐射鲁棒性的论证。

Conclusion: 结论指出，非对易时空的非局域性使传统霍金辐射鲁棒性论证失效，辐射过程的显著衰减导致黑洞蒸发时间大幅延长，这对理解量子引力效应下的黑洞热力学具有重要意义。

Abstract: We investigate Hawking radiation in noncommutative spacetime. For a dynamical black hole formed by the collapse of a matter shell, we demonstrate that spacetime noncommutativity modifies the interaction between the radiation field and the background geometry. In particular, the collapsing shell is effectively shifted by an amount proportional to the momentum of an outgoing Hawking mode. While the nonlocality inherent in noncommutative spacetime invalidates the conventional arguments for the robustness of Hawking radiation, the radiation decays substantially after the scrambling time, resulting in an exponentially long evaporation time.

</details>


### [191] [Planar AdS multi-NUT spacetimes and Kaluza-Klein multi-monopoles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.04817)
*Cristóbal Corral,Cristián Erices,Daniel Flores-Alfonso,Benjamín Hernández*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文在高维爱因斯坦-反德西特引力中，通过两种方法构造了具有多个NUT参数的平面AdS时空，突破了真空场方程的严格限制，为研究具有多个NUT电荷的全息性质铺平了道路。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 论文采用两种简单方法构造具有多个NUT参数的平面AdS时空：首先，受动量弛豫全息模型启发，通过添加具有轴子轮廓的自由标量场构造平直视界的多NUT空间；其次，在具有二次曲率修正的爱因斯坦引力中构建类似配置。

Result: 成功构造了具有多个NUT参数的显式平面AdS时空，突破了真空场方程的严格限制，并作为副产品给出了具有不同磁荷的AdS中卡鲁扎-克莱因磁单极子的平面版本。

Conclusion: 该研究为研究具有多个NUT电荷的全息性质开辟了新方向，通过引入额外场或修正引力理论成功克服了传统方法的局限性。

Abstract: In higher-dimensional Einstein-AdS gravity, it is well known that planar and static anti-de Sitter black holes can be endowed with multiple rotation parameters via a large-gauge transformation. However, a similar prescription fails when multiple NUT parameters are added, thereby obstructing the study of holographic properties with more than one NUT charge. To pave the way towards this direction, we construct explicit planar AdS spacetimes having multiple NUT parameters in two simple ways that allow one to circumvent the strong restrictions imposed by the vacuum field equations. First, motivated by momentum relaxation holographic models, we construct multi-NUT spaces in AdS with flat horizons by adding free scalar fields possessing an axionic profile. In our second approach, we build similar configurations in Einstein gravity with quadratic-curvature corrections. As a byproduct, we end by presenting planar versions of the Kaluza-Klein monopole in AdS with different magnetic charges.

### [192] [Symmetries of non-maximal supergravities with higher-derivative corrections](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.21459)
*Yi Pang,Robert J. Saskowski*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究了非极大高阶导数超引力（non-maximal higher-derivative supergravities）在三维约化中由U-对偶（U-duality）产生的隐藏对称性（hidden symmetries），发现高阶导数修正会明确破坏所有隐藏对称性增强。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探讨非极大高阶导数超引力在三维约化过程中，U-对偶所产生的隐藏对称性如何受到高阶导数修正的影响。特别关注最小五维超引力（minimal five-dimensional supergravity）的$G_{2(2)}$对称性和玻色/杂化弦理论（bosonic and heterotic string theory）在$T^d$上的$O(d+p+1,d+1)$对称性。

Method: 采用群论论证（group theory argument）方法，分析高阶导数修正对隐藏对称性增强的影响。具体考察了最小五维超引力和玻色/杂化弦理论在环面紧致化（compactification on $T^d$）下的对称性结构。

Result: 研究结果表明，高阶导数修正明确破坏了所有隐藏对称性增强。作为特例，这还意味着高阶导数修正阻止了纯五维引力（pure five-dimensional gravity）中向$SL(3,\mathbb R)$的对称性增强，以及STU模型中向$O(4,4)$的对称性增强。

Conclusion: 高阶导数修正对隐藏对称性具有破坏性影响，即使在三维约化过程中由U-对偶产生的对称性增强也会被明确破坏。这一结论对理解高阶导数项在超引力理论和弦理论对称性结构中的作用具有重要意义。

Abstract: We consider hidden symmetries arising from U-duality in the dimensional reduction of non-maximal higher-derivative supergravities to three dimensions. In particular, we consider the $G_{2(2)}$ symmetry of minimal five-dimensional supergravity and the $O(d+p+1,d+1)$ symmetry of bosonic and heterotic string theory on $T^d$. Using a group theory argument, we show that the higher-derivative corrections explicitly break all hidden symmetry enhancements. As special cases, this also implies that higher-derivative corrections prevent the symmetry enhancement to $SL(3,\mathbb R)$ in pure five-dimensional gravity and $O(4,4)$ in the STU model.

</details>

### [193] [Dose Validation of GRID Block Treatment Applicator within the RayStation Treatment Planning System](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.03967)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Spatially Fractionated Radiation Therapy (SFRT) or GRID therapy has been in existence for more than a century. A few TPS software vendors such as Elekta and Varian have protocols for treating patients with GRID therapy. However, we are the first to implement the protocols within RayStation TPS. To achieve these, we used the .decimal GRID block applicator to create conformal treatment plans. For the beam modeling, several dosimetry data, and measurements such as percentage depth dose (PDD), beam profile, output, and GRID factors, were obtained for different field sizes and energies. The dose distribution from the GRID openings covered the Planning Target Volume (PTV), with the QA plan having a 98% agreement with the planned dose. Also, we used the Mapcheck2 results to verify the adjustments made to the script variables such as aperture size (hole and spacing). We developed a robust way to validate the dose needed for patient treatment using the GRID block applicator. Also, we have proposed a novel approach to standardize the clinical implementation of the GRID block in RayStation TPS.

### [194] [Lattice simulations of scalar-induced gravitational waves from inflation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.03628)
*Angelo Caravano,Gabriele Franciolini,Sébastien Renaux-Petel*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 该研究通过晶格模拟（lattice simulations）计算了超慢滚（ultra-slow-roll）暴胀情景中由标量诱导的引力波（SIGWs），发现当暴胀非高斯性（non-Gaussianities）较大时，传统的半解析预测在振幅和谱形上都会显著失效。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在具有瞬态超慢滚（ultra-slow-roll, USR）相的暴胀情景中，曲率功率谱在小尺度上可能被强烈增强，从而产生可观测的随机引力波背景。然而，该区域的标量动力学可能变得非线性，挑战了标准微扰预测的有效性，而现有的半解析计算依赖于暴胀涨落的线性演化。

Method: 采用晶格模拟（lattice simulations）方法，在暴胀期间完全非线性地演化暴胀子场，并以非微扰方式提取曲率扰动。随后通过线性演化牛顿势来模拟再加热后的视界重入，同时保留张量源中原始涨落初始条件的完整非高斯结构。

Result: 对于中等程度的非高斯性，半解析预测能捕捉到引力波信号正确的数量级，但需要重要修正。当暴胀非高斯性（non-Gaussianities）较大时，半解析预测在振幅和谱形上都会显著失效，且这种失效与张量功率谱的整体大小无关。

Conclusion: 研究结果表明，在此类情景中要获得标量诱导引力波（SIGWs）的可靠预测，需要对暴胀标量动力学进行非微扰控制。相关代码已在GitHub上开源。

Abstract: Scalar-induced gravitational waves (SIGWs) provide a powerful probe of inflationary dynamics on scales far smaller than those accessible to the cosmic microwave background and large-scale structure. In scenarios with a transient ultra-slow-roll (USR) phase, the curvature power spectrum can be strongly enhanced on small scales, potentially generating an observable stochastic GW background. In this regime, scalar dynamics during inflation can become nonlinear, challenging the validity of standard perturbative predictions. Existing semi-analytical calculations of SIGWs rely on the linear evolution of inflation fluctuations. In this work, we compute SIGWs from USR inflation using lattice simulations. We evolve the inflaton field fully nonlinearly during inflation and extract the curvature perturbation nonperturbatively, then simulate its post-reheating horizon re-entry by evolving the Newtonian potential linearly while retaining the full non-Gaussian structure of the initial conditions for the primordial fluctuations in the tensor source. For moderate non-Gaussianity, the semi-analytical prediction captures the correct order of magnitude of the GW signal but receives important corrections. When inflationary non-Gaussianities are large, it can fail dramatically in both amplitude and spectral shape, independently of the overall size of the tensor power spectrum. Our results show that reliable predictions of SIGWs in such scenarios require nonperturbative control of the inflationary scalar dynamics. The code used for this work is available at https://github.com/caravangelo/inflation-easy.git.

</details>


### [195] [Is the $w_0w_a$CDM cosmological parameterization evidence for dark energy dynamics partially caused by the excess smoothing of Planck PR4 CMB anisotropy data?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.03756)
*Chan-Gyung Park,Javier de Cruz Perez,Bharat Ratra*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 该研究比较了平坦ΛCDM模型与两种动力学暗能量参数化模型（w₀CDM和w₀wₐCDM）在不同数据集下的表现，评估了Planck PR3与PR4数据的约束稳定性，发现PR4数据轻微倾向于时间演化的暗能量，但部分偏好可能与PR4 CMB谱中可能的残余过度平滑有关。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在评估平坦ΛCDM模型与动力学暗能量参数化模型的性能，并比较Planck PR3与PR4数据对宇宙学约束的稳定性。特别关注CMB透镜一致性参数A_L的变化如何影响暗能量性质的推断。

Method: 研究采用Planck PR4 CMB数据（包括透镜数据）与非CMB数据组合，后者包含重子声学振荡（BAO）数据（不含DESI BAO）、Pantheon+ Ia型超新星观测、哈勃参数测量H(z)和增长率fσ₈数据。通过对比PR3与PR4数据结果来评估约束稳定性。

Result: 对于最大数据组合，PR3与PR4推断的宇宙学参数基本一致（差异在1σ以内）。在ΛCDM+A_L模型中，PR4数据的A_L=1.053±0.034（高于单位值1.6σ），表明CMB透镜异常有所减弱。在w₀wₐCDM参数化中，发现w₀=-0.863±0.060（类quintessence）且w₀+wₐ=-1.37^{+0.19}_{-0.17}（类phantom），当前观测以约1.8σ水平倾向于动力学暗能量而非宇宙学常数。

Conclusion: PR4数据轻微倾向于时间演化的暗能量，但部分偏好可能与Planck PR4 CMB各向异性谱中可能的残余过度平滑有关。CMB透镜异常在使用PR4数据时有所减弱，但动力学暗能量的证据仍需进一步验证。

Abstract: We study the performance of the flat $Λ$CDM model and the dynamical dark energy parameterizations $w_0$CDM and $w_0w_a$CDM, in which the dark energy (DE) equation of state is either constant ($w=w_0$) or redshift-dependent [$w(z)=w_0+w_a z/(1+z)$], without and with a varying CMB lensing consistency parameter $A_L$, using combinations of Planck PR4 CMB data (PR4 and lensing), and a compilation of non-CMB data composed of baryon acoustic oscillation (BAO) data that do not include DESI BAO data, Pantheon+ type Ia supernova observations, Hubble parameter measurements $H(z)$, and growth rate $fσ_8$ data. We also compare results from earlier Planck PR3 data with those obtained using PR4 data in order to assess the stability of cosmological constraints. For the largest data combinations, PR3/PR4+lensing+non-CMB, the cosmological parameters inferred from PR3 and PR4 data are consistent, almost all differing by $1σ$ or less. For the $Λ$CDM$+A_L$ model, we have $A_L=1.087 \pm 0.035$ for PR3 and $A_L=1.053 \pm 0.034$ ($1.6σ$ above unity) for PR4, which indicates that the CMB lensing anomaly is reduced when PR4 data are used. For the $w_0 w_a$CDM parameterization, we find $w_0 = -0.863\pm0.060$ (quintessence-like) and $w_0+w_a=-1.37^{+0.19}_{-0.17}$ (phantom-like), suggesting that the current observations favor dynamical DE over a cosmological constant at about $1.8σ$. For the $w_0w_a$CDM$+A_L$ parameterization, we find $w_0=-0.877\pm 0.060$ and $w_0 + w_a =-1.29_{-0.17}^{+0.20}$, corresponding to a preference for dynamical DE over a cosmological constant of about $1.5σ$ and with $A_L = 1.042 \pm 0.037$ exceeding unity at $1.1σ$. These results indicate that while the PR4 data mildly favor a time-evolving DE, part of this preference may be associated with possible residual excess smoothing present in the Planck PR4 CMB anisotropy spectra (abridged).

</details>


### [196] [Dispersion Measure Distribution of Unlocalized Fast Radio Bursts as a Probe of the Hubble Constant](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.03769)
*Yang Liu,Jun-Jie Wei,Puxun Wu,Xue-Feng Wu*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 该研究首次利用未定位快速射电暴（FRB）的色散量（DM）分布独立约束哈勃常数（H_0），获得H_0 = 73.8^{+14.0}_{-12.3} km s^{-1} Mpc^{-1}（1σ置信度），不确定性约18%，展示了未定位FRB作为新宇宙学探针的潜力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 虽然已定位且有红移测量的快速射电暴（FRB）已被用于研究哈勃张力（Hubble tension），但其样本量有限。该研究旨在利用数量远多于前者的未定位FRB，在不依赖红移信息的情况下独立约束哈勃常数，因为宇宙膨胀效应会印刻在它们的色散量（DM）分布上。

Method: 研究分析了来自CHIME Catalog II的2124个未定位快速射电暴（FRB）的选定样本，通过其色散量（dispersion measure, DM）分布来约束哈勃常数（H_0）。该方法利用了宇宙膨胀对DM分布的印记效应，无需单个FRB的红移信息。

Result: 在1σ置信度下获得哈勃常数H_0 = 73.8^{+14.0}_{-12.3} km s^{-1} Mpc^{-1}，对应不确定性约18%。研究指出，若能打破H_0与FRB各向同性能量分布的特征截止能量E_*之间的简并性，可将不确定性降低至9%。

Conclusion: 这是首个仅从未定位快速射电暴（FRB）的色散量（DM）分布推导出的H_0测量结果，突显了未定位FRB作为新宇宙学探针的潜力。未来与已定位FRB的联合分析有望提供更严格的约束。

Abstract: We present constraints on the Hubble constant ($H_0$) derived from the observed dispersion measure (DM) distribution of unlocalized fast radio bursts (FRBs). While localized FRBs with redshift measurements have been used to investigate the Hubble tension, their sample remains limited. Here we demonstrate that unlocalized FRBs -- which are far more numerous -- can independently constrain $H_0$ without requiring redshift information, as cosmic expansion imprints itself on their DM distribution. Analyzing a selected sample of 2124 unlocalized FRBs from the CHIME Catalog II, we obtain $H_0 = 73.8^{+14.0}_{-12.3}~\mathrm{km\,s^{-1}\,Mpc^{-1}}$ at the $1σ$ confidence level, corresponding to an uncertainty of about 18%. Breaking the degeneracy between $H_0$ and the characteristic cutoff energy $E_*$ of the FRB isotropic energy distribution would reduce this uncertainty to 9%. This work constitutes the first $H_0$ measurement derived solely from the DM distribution of unlocalized FRBs, highlighting their potential as a new cosmological probe. Future joint analyses with localized FRBs promise even tighter constraints.

### [197] [Fidelity and quantum geometry approach to Dirac exceptional points in diamond nitrogen-vacancy centers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.00666)
*Chia-Yi Ju,Gunnar Möller,Yu-Chin Tzeng*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该研究理论探讨了金刚石氮空位中心中狄拉克例外点（Dirac exceptional points）的量子几何特性，利用保真度磁化率（fidelity susceptibility）作为探针，揭示了其各向异性的发散行为，与传统例外点的全向发散形成鲜明对比。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 狄拉克例外点（Dirac exceptional points）作为一类新型非厄米奇点，完全位于宇称-时间对称未破缺相内并展现线性能量色散。研究旨在探索这类奇点的量子几何特性，验证保真度在表征非厄米例外点方面的有效性。

Method: 采用理论研究方法，以金刚石氮空位中心（nitrogen-vacancy centers）为平台实现狄拉克例外点，利用保真度磁化率（fidelity susceptibility）作为探针来表征量子几何特性。

Result: 研究证实狄拉克例外点诱导显著的几何奇点，保真度磁化率的实部发散至负无穷，可作为非厄米临界性的特征。关键发现是这种发散具有明显各向异性：沿非互易耦合方向发散，而沿失谐轴保持有限。这种各向异性是狄拉克例外点结构的普遍结果，其特征是至少存在一个精确暗方向与发散方向共存。

Conclusion: 研究结果提供了狄拉克例外点附近保真度探针的完整图像，强调了参数方向性在利用狄拉克例外点进行量子控制和传感应用中的关键作用。狄拉克例外点的各向异性发散行为与传统例外点的全向发散形成鲜明对比。

Abstract: Dirac exceptional points (EPs) represent a novel class of non-Hermitian singularities that, unlike conventional EPs, reside entirely within the parity-time unbroken phase and exhibit linear energy dispersion. Here, we theoretically investigate the quantum geometry of Dirac EPs realized in nitrogen-vacancy centers in diamond, utilizing fidelity susceptibility as a probe. We demonstrate that despite the absence of a symmetry-breaking phase transition, the Dirac EP induces a pronounced geometric singularity, confirming the validity of the fidelity in characterizing non-Hermitian EPs. Specifically, the real part of the fidelity susceptibility diverges to negative infinity, which serves as a signature of non-Hermitian criticality. Crucially, however, we reveal that this divergence exhibits a distinct anisotropy, diverging along the non-reciprocal coupling direction while remaining finite along the detuning axis. Furthermore, we establish that this anisotropy, characterized by at least one exact dark direction coexisting with divergent directions, is a generic consequence of the Dirac EP structure whenever the parameter derivatives collectively span the off-diagonal operator space at the Dirac EP. This behavior stands in stark contrast to the omnidirectional divergence observed in conventional EPs. Our findings provide a comprehensive picture of the fidelity probe near the Dirac EP, highlighting the critical role of parameter directionality in exploiting Dirac EPs for quantum control and sensing applications.

</details>


### [198] [Quantum Realization of the Wallis Formula](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.03662)
*Bin Ye,Ruitao Chen,Lei Yin*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文从量子力学角度统一推导了沃利斯公式（Wallis formula），通过两个可解径向系统：三维各向同性谐振子的圆形态和平面福克-达尔文问题的低径向分支态。当角动量较大时，两个系统的有限乘积表示均收敛于π的沃利斯公式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在从量子力学角度统一推导沃利斯公式（Wallis formula），该公式是π的经典无穷乘积表示。通过分析两个具有精确径向概率密度的可解系统，探索量子力学与经典数学公式之间的深刻联系。

Method: 采用两个可解径向系统：三维各向同性谐振子的圆形态（circular states）和平面福克-达尔文问题（Fock--Darwin problem）的低径向分支态，包括最低朗道能级（lowest Landau level）区域。两个系统的径向概率密度均具有精确形式 $P(r)\propto r^νe^{-λr^2}$，由此导出尺度无关的倒数可观测量 $Q=\langle r\rangle\langle r^{-1}\rangle$。

Result: 两个系统分别实现了相同矩公式的偶数和奇数半整数伽马函数分支（Gamma-function branches）。相应的有限沃利斯部分乘积（finite Wallis partial products）在一个情况下由$Q$决定，在另一个情况下由$Q^{-1}$决定。在大角动量区域，对应态局域于薄球壳或窄环上，相对径向宽度趋近于零，导致$Q\to1$，两个有限乘积表示均简化为π的沃利斯公式。

Conclusion: 研究成功建立了量子力学系统与经典数学公式之间的直接联系，通过两个可解径向系统统一推导了沃利斯公式。该方法揭示了量子态的大角动量极限如何自然地产生π的经典无穷乘积表示，为理解量子力学与数学常数之间的关系提供了新视角。

Abstract: We present a unified quantum-mechanical derivation of the Wallis formula from two solvable radial systems: the circular states of the three-dimensional isotropic harmonic oscillator and the lowest-radial-branch states of the planar Fock--Darwin problem, including the lowest Landau level sector. In both cases, the radial probability density has the exact form $P(r)\propto r^νe^{-λr^2}$, which yields the scale-independent reciprocal observable $Q=\langle r\rangle\langle r^{-1}\rangle$. The two systems realize the even and odd half-integer Gamma-function branches of the same moment formula, so that the associated finite Wallis partial products are determined by $Q$ in one case and by $Q^{-1}$ in the other. In the large-angular-momentum regime, the corresponding states become localized on a thin spherical shell or a narrow annulus, with vanishing relative radial width, so that $Q\to1$ and both finite-product representations reduce to the Wallis formula for $π$.

</details>


### [199] [Three Hamiltonians are Sufficient for Unitary $k$-Design in Temporal Ensemble](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.04205)
*Yi-Neng Zhou,Tian-Gang Zhou,Julian Sonner*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该研究证明，通过三次淬灭协议（3SP）的时间随机性可以生成任意k阶酉设计（unitary k-design），而二次淬灭协议（2SP）则无法实现一般酉设计。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 酉k设计（unitary k-design）是量子信息和量子多体物理中作为Haar随机动力学高效代理的核心工具。研究旨在探索如何通过混沌哈密顿演化生成酉设计，避免传统方法对多个独立哈密顿实现或精细调节演化时间的依赖。

Method: 提出基于淬灭时间系综（quenched temporal ensemble）的方法，其中哈密顿量采样一次并固定，随机性仅通过演化时间引入。分析二次淬灭协议（2SP）和三次淬灭协议（3SP），所有时间从规定分布中随机抽取。使用框架势（frame potential，FP）量化与Haar随机的距离。

Result: 分析表明2SP无法实现一般酉k设计，而3SP可以生成任意k阶酉设计。3SP的优势在于额外的随机相位施加了更强的约束，消除了框架势中独立的置换自由度。对于高斯酉系综哈密顿量，严格证明了这些结果，并显示在不完美时间平均下，3SP能以参数更窄的时间窗口达到与2SP相同的精度。

Conclusion: 淬灭时间系综提供了一种生成酉设计的新方法，其中三次淬灭协议通过额外的随机相位约束能够实现任意阶酉设计，相比二次协议具有显著优势，为量子信息处理提供了更高效的随机性生成机制。

Abstract: Unitary $k$-designs are central to quantum information and quantum many-body physics as efficient proxies for Haar-random dynamics. We study how chaotic Hamiltonian evolution can generate unitary $k$-designs. Standard approaches typically rely on many independent Hamiltonian realizations or fine-tuning evolution times. Here we show that unitary designs can instead arise from a quenched temporal ensemble, where Hamiltonians are sampled once and held fixed, while randomness enters only through the evolution times. We analyze a two-step protocol (2SP), applying $H_1$ for time $t_1$ and $H_2$ for time $t_2$, and a three-step protocol (3SP) with an additional quench, with all times randomly drawn from a prescribed distribution. Time averaging imposes energy-index matching in the frame potential (FP), which quantifies the distance to Haar random. Analytically and numerically, we show that 2SP cannot realize a general unitary $k$-design, whereas 3SP can do so for arbitrary $k$. The advantage of 3SP is that the additional random phases impose stronger constraints, eliminating independent permutation degrees of freedom in the FP. For Gaussian unitary ensemble Hamiltonians, we prove these results rigorously and show that under imperfect time averaging, 3SP achieves the same accuracy as 2SP with a parametrically narrower time window.

</details>


### [200] [Optimal, Qubit-Efficient Quantum Vehicle Routing via Colored-Permutations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.04570)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出全局位置着色排列编码（global-position colored-permutation encoding），其中K辆车选择不相交的部分排列，这K个颜色层的和构成完整的n×n排列矩阵。该方法使用n²K个二进制决策变量，排列在公共排列结构上的K个颜色层中，通过每个颜色类条目的加权和来强制执行车辆容量约束，无需显式负载寄存器。

Result: 该编码在量子比特效率方面表现优异，同时在算法性能上也表现强劲。在标准基准测试套件上，端到端管道恢复了独立验证的最优解。可行性预言机（feasibility oracle）作为可重用的多项式时间解码和认证原语，对量子和量子启发式路由管道具有独立价值。

Conclusion: 所提出的编码方法旨在与约束增强QAOA框架及其编码流形分析相结合，基于CVRP中量子效用的需求视角，直接针对近期主要瓶颈之一——车辆标签和显式容量约束的额外逻辑量子比特成本，提供了高效的解决方案。

Abstract: We formulate a global-position colored-permutation encoding for the capacitated vehicle routing problem. Each of the $K$ vehicles selects a disjoint partial permutation, and the sum of these $K$ color layers forms a full $n\times n$ permutation matrix that assigns every customer to exactly one visit position. This representation uses $n^2K$ binary decision variables arranged as $K$ color layers over a common permutation structure, while vehicle capacities are enforced by weighted sums over the entries of each color class, requiring no explicit load register and hence no extra logical qubits beyond the routing variables. In contrast, many prior quantum encodings introduce an explicit capacity or load representation with additional qubits. Our construction is designed to exploit the Constraint-Enhanced QAOA framework together with its encoded-manifold analyses. Building on a requirements-based view of quantum utility in CVRP, we develop a routing optimization formulation that directly targets one of the main near-term bottlenecks, namely the additional logical-qubit cost of vehicle labels and explicit capacity constraints. Our proposal shows strong algorithmic performance in addition to qubit efficiency. On a standard benchmark suite, our end-to-end pipeline recovers the independently verified optima. The feasibility oracle may also be of independent interest as a reusable polynomial-time decoding and certification primitive for quantum and quantum-inspired routing pipelines.

### [201] [Nonlocal advantage of quantum imaginarity in Schwarzchild spacetime](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.03633)
*Bing Yu,Xiao-Yong Yang,Xiao-Li Hu,Zhi-Xiang Jin,Xiao-Fen Huang*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了霍金辐射对史瓦西时空（Schwarzschild spacetime）中量子虚性（quantum imaginarity）的影响，重点分析了非局域量子虚性优势（NAQI）和辅助虚性蒸馏（assisted imaginarity distillation）在黑洞时空中的行为。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究在史瓦西时空背景下，分析非局域量子虚性优势（NAQI）和辅助虚性蒸馏两种量子虚性度量。重点关注霍金温度变化对这些度量的影响，并区分物理可访问区域（physically accessible region）和物理不可访问区域（physically inaccessible region）的不同行为。

Result: 对于NAQI，霍金辐射对其有显著影响，物理可访问区域和不可访问区域表现出明显差异：在可访问区域，NAQI随霍金温度升高而受到抑制甚至消失；而在不可访问区域，在整个参数范围内NAQI均不存在。对于辅助虚性蒸馏，霍金效应以状态依赖的方式改变辅助保真度（assisted fidelity）：在可访问区域，保真度随温度升高而降低，表明蒸馏能力减弱；而在不可访问区域则呈现相反的单调趋势，表明蒸馏能力增强。

Conclusion: 这些结果突显了在相对论效应下，物理可访问区域和不可访问区域具有不同的操作行为，为理解弯曲时空中的量子虚性提供了重要见解。研究揭示了霍金辐射对量子虚性度量的复杂影响模式。

Abstract: Black hole spacetimes provide a natural setting for quantum systems in curved spacetime, where effects such as Hawking radiation arise from event horizons. In this work, we investigate the impact of the Hawking effect on quantum imaginarity in Schwarzschild spacetime, focusing on nonlocal advantage of quantum imaginarity (NAQI) and assisted imaginarity distillation. For NAQI, it is significantly affected by Hawking radiation, exhibiting a pronounced difference between physically accessible and inaccessible regions. It is suppressed in the physically accessible region with increasing Hawking temperature and may vanish, while remaining absent in the physically inaccessible region across the parameter regime. For assisted imaginarity distillation, the Hawking effect modifies the assisted fidelity in a state-dependent manner. In the physically accessible region, the fidelity generally decreases with increasing temperature, indicating reduced distillation capability, whereas the physically inaccessible region exhibits the opposite monotonic trend, indicating enhanced distillation capability. These results highlight distinct operational behaviors of physically accessible and inaccessible regions under relativistic effects, providing insight into quantum imaginarity in curved spacetime.

  <summary>Details</summary>
