Method: 通过交流电场（ac electric field）驱动的多电子中介量子点（multielectron mediator quantum dot）实现电容耦合（capacitive coupling），以谐振交换量子比特（resonant exchange qubits）为例，该量子比特由三电子三量子点（three-electron triple quantum dots）定义，具有固有的自旋-电荷混合（spin-charge mixing）特性。

Abstract: We present an approach for entangling spin qubits via capacitive coupling mediated by an ac electric field-driven multielectron mediator quantum dot. To illustrate this method, we consider the case of a driven two-electron dot that mediates entanglement between resonant exchange qubits defined in three-electron triple quantum dots, which enable direct capacitive coupling and interaction with microwave fields via intrinsic spin-charge mixing. The method can also be applied to other types of spin qubits that can be coupled capacitively. We show that this approach leads to rapid, single-pulse universal entangling gates for resonant exchange qubits that are activated via the drive on the mediator dot. Unlike conventional tunneling-based two-qubit gates between exchange-only qubits, the capacitive interaction-based gates we describe do not require an extensive sequence of pulses to mitigate leakage. We describe how this drive-activated local entangling approach can be integrated with the driven sideband-based long-range approach for cavity-mediated entangling gates developed in our previous work in order to enable modularity for spin-based quantum information processing.

Abstract: Periodic (Floquet) driving enables Hamiltonian engineering and nonequilibrium phases, but interacting systems eventually heat by absorbing energy from the drive. Disorder can greatly delay this process, yielding long-lived prethermal plateaus. Here we show that this protection can fail when pulse-train control introduces a second driving frequency and when the disorder fluctuates. Using a natural-abundance 13C nuclear-spin network in diamond, we observe sharp peaks in the late-time heating rate at the double- and triple-spin-flip resonance conditions predicted by bimodal Floquet interference, and track their evolution with drive frequency. ### [204] [Moving Detector Quantum Walk with Random Relocation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.03593)
*Md Aquib Molla,Sanchari Goswami*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该研究分析了在随机重定位探测器存在下的离散时间量子行走（discrete-time quantum walk）。比较了两种探测器重定位模型：无限制重定位（Model 1）和窗口限制重定位（Model 2），重点考察了探测器移除时间（removal time）对行走者扩散行为的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索量子行走（quantum walk）在随机重定位探测器影响下的动力学行为。通过比较两种不同的探测器重定位规则，旨在理解探测器移除时间（removal time）和重定位策略如何影响量子行走者的扩散特性。

Method: 研究方法基于离散时间量子行走（discrete-time quantum walk），在位置$x_D$处初始设置探测器。探测器在移除时间$t_R$后被移除，并随机重定位。比较两种模型：Model 1允许在$x_D$之外的任意位置重定位；Model 2限制在探测器当前位置周围的有限窗口内重定位。

Result: 当$t_R$较大时，两种模型均表现出类似半无限行走（Semi Infinite Walk, SIW）的行为，探测器等效于固定边界。在快速重定位（rapid-relocation）区域（$t_R$较小），两种模型行为差异显著：Model 1由于无限制重定位允许更大的扩散。占据概率比$f(x_D,t)/f_\infty(x_D,t)$的时间演化显示，初始呈现SIW特征，随后出现振荡，最终达到饱和值。饱和比在移除时间$t_R^*$上下呈现交叉（crossover）行为。

Conclusion: 研究揭示了随机重定位探测器对量子行走动力学的显著影响。两种重定位模型在快速重定位区域表现出截然不同的行为，与半无限行走（SIW）、淬灭量子行走（Quenched Quantum Walk, QQW）和移动探测器量子行走（Moving Detector Quantum Walk, MDQW）均有明显区别。特定条件下占据概率比的增强是纯粹的量子力学效应，相关比（correlation ratios）显示出与初始探测器位置相关的有趣时间依赖性。

Abstract: We study a discrete-time quantum walk in presence of a detector at $x_D$ initially. The detector here is repeatedly removed after a span of $t_R$, the removal time, and reinserted at random locations. Two relocation rules are considered here: In Model~1, the detector is reinserted at any site beyond $x_D$, while in Model~2, reinsertion is done within a restricted window around the position of the detector at that time. Both variants behave like Semi Infinite Walk (SIW) for large $t_R$, where the detector behaves effectively as a fixed boundary. However, in the rapid-relocation regime, i.e., when $t_R$ is small, the behaviours are different. Model~1 permits greater spreading due to unrestricted reinsertion, which is different from Model~2. The time evolution of occupation probability ratio of our walker to that of an infinite walker at $x_D$, i.e., $f(x_D,t)/f_\infty(x_D,t)$, initially show the feature of a SIW upto $t=t_R$, then show some oscillatory behaviour and finally reach a saturation value for both the models. The ratio enhancing under certain conditions of $x_D$ and $t_R$, is a purely quantum mechanical effect. The saturation ratio shows a crossover behavior below and above a removal time $t_R^*$. At sites $x \neq x_D$ the occupation probablity ratios at a certain time reveals that for small $t_R$, the behaviours of the two models are drastically different from each other, as well as from Semi Infinite Walk (SIW), Quenched Quantum Walk (QQW) and Moving Detector Quantum Walk (MDQW). The correlation ratios of the two models with that of Infinite Walk (IW) show interesting time dependence for sites to the left or right of the initial detector position $x_D$.

### [205] [Microstructural Topology as a Prescriptor for Quantum Coherence: Towards A Unified Framework for Decoherence in Superconducting Qubits](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.03951)
*Vinayak P. Dravid,Akshay A. Murthy,Peter Lim,Gabriel T. dos Santos,Ramandeep Mandia,James M. Rondinelli,Mark C. Hersam,Roberto dos Reis*

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种用于超导transmon量子比特退相干（decoherence）分析的可分离框架，将微结构状态变量与几何依赖耦合函数分离，建立了五类主导损耗通道的描述符（prescriptor），并制定了可证伪性实验协议。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超导量子电路中，退相干改进通常涉及同时改变表面化学、微观结构拓扑和器件几何的工艺干预，导致机制归因在结构上无法确定。预测性材料工程需要将可测量的结构统计量与几何依赖的耦合系数分离为可独立测试的因子。

Method: 论文引入了经典和量子微观结构（classical and quantum microstructure）概念，并构建了通道可分离框架，其中每个损耗通道由简化描述符（reduced prescriptor）描述。该框架从空间分辨核表示（spatially resolved kernel representation）推导出乘积形式，并建立了微扰可分离性准则（perturbative separability criterion）。

Result: 该框架为transmon类器件中的主导损耗通道指定了五类描述符。通过预承诺的2x2实验协议（pre-committed 2x2 experimental protocol）实现可证伪性，其中变量必须在传播不确定性内满足独立比率检查。最小数据集规范（Minimum-Dataset Specification）标准化了跨实验室推断的报告。

Conclusion: 第一部分建立了概念和数学架构，协调的实验验证保留给第二部分。该框架将微结构状态变量与几何依赖耦合函数分离，使独立变化有效，为预测性材料工程提供了可测试的理论基础。

Abstract: In superconducting quantum circuits, decoherence improvements are frequently obtained through process interventions that simultaneously modify surface chemistry, microstructural topology, and device geometry, leaving mechanistic attribution structurally underdetermined. Predictive materials engineering requires measurable structural statistics to be separated from geometry-dependent coupling coefficients into independently testable factors. We introduce the concept of classical and quantum microstructure. In that context, we formulate a channel-wise separable framework for decoherence in superconducting transmon qubits in which each loss channel is described by a reduced prescriptor. Here, a channel-specific microstructural state variable is determined independently of device geometry, and a geometry-dependent coupling functional is computable from field solutions without reference to surface chemistry. We derive this product form from a spatially resolved kernel representation and establish a perturbative separability criterion that defines the regime where independent variation of the variables is valid. The framework specifies five prescriptor classes for dominant loss pathways in transmon-class devices. Falsifiability is operationalized through a pre-committed 2x2 experimental protocol in which the variables must satisfy independent ratio checks within propagated uncertainty. A Minimum-Dataset Specification standardizes reporting for cross-laboratory inference. Part I establishes the conceptual and mathematical architecture; coordinated experimental validation is reserved for Part II.

</details>


### [206] [Dismagicker: Unitary Gate for Non-Stabilizerness Reduction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.04046)
*Jiale Huang,Rongyi Lv,Xiangjian Qian,Mingpu Qin*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了"dismagicker"概念——一种非克利福德（non-Clifford）幺正门，旨在降低量子多体态的非稳定子性（non-stabilizerness，又称"魔力"）。该工作将非稳定子性抑制与纠缠降低统一起来，显著提升了多体系统的经典模拟精度和量子设备上的态制备效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 虽然纠缠（entanglement）和非稳定子性都是基本的量子资源，但它们需要不同的控制策略。在张量网络方法中，降低纠缠的幺正操作（disentanglers）已很成熟，但针对非稳定子性抑制的类似概念却基本缺失。本研究旨在填补这一空白。

Method: 本文定义了dismagicker作为主动抑制非稳定子性的非克利福德幺正操作，将量子态导向经典可模拟的稳定子态（stabilizer states）。在矩阵乘积态（Matrix Product States）框架内开发了构建dismagicker的优化方法。

Result: 数值结果表明，非稳定子性降低过程与克利福德电路（Clifford circuits）的纠缠降低步骤相结合，显著提高了多体系统经典模拟和量子设备上量子态制备的准确性。

Conclusion: Dismagicker通过统一非稳定子性和纠缠降低，丰富了多体态操作的工具体系。该概念为量子资源管理提供了新的理论框架和实用工具。

Abstract: We introduce the notion of dismagicker: non-Clifford unitary gate designed to reduce the non-stabilizerness (also called magic) of quantum many-body states. Although both entanglement and non-stabilizerness are fundamental quantum resources, they require distinct control strategies. While disentanglers (unitary operations that lower entanglement) are well-established in tensor network methods, analogous concept for non-stabilizerness suppression has been largely missing. In this work, we define dismagicker as non-Clifford unitary operation that actively suppresses non-stabilizerness, steering states toward classically simulatable stabilizer states. We develop optimization method for constructing dismagickers within the Matrix Product States framework. Our numerical results show that the non-stabilizerness reduction procedure, when combined with entanglement reduction steps with Clifford circuits, significantly improves the accuracy for both classical simulation of many-body systems and quantum state preparation on quantum devices. Dismagicker enriches our toolkit for the manipulation of many-body states by unifying non-stabilizerness and entanglement reduction.

### [207] [Noise tolerance via reinforcement in the quantum search problem](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.04137)
*Marjan Homayouni-Sangari,Abolfazl Ramezanpour*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该研究发现强化（reinforcement）能将量子搜索问题的计算时间从√D指数级减少到lnD，从而在噪声环境中显著提高算法的噪声容限阈值。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在解决量子搜索算法在噪声环境中的性能问题，特别是当精确噪声模型不可用时，需要有效的错误缓解策略。

Method: 采用数值模拟方法，在包含相干噪声（coherent noise）和非相干噪声（incoherent noise）的环境中，分别对N个量子比特（qubits）系统和单个D能级（qudit）系统进行强化量子搜索的特性分析。

Result: 强化显著提高了算法的成功概率，并改善了计算时间随系统尺寸的标度关系，使量子搜索在噪声环境中展现出指数级更大的噪声阈值。

Conclusion: 强化提供了一种有前景的错误缓解策略，特别是在缺乏精确噪声模型的情况下，能够有效增强量子算法的鲁棒性。

Abstract: We find that reinforcement exponentially reduces computation time of the quantum search problem from $\sqrt{D}$ to $\ln D$ in a $D$-dimensional system. Therefor, a reinforced quantum search is expected to exhibit an exponentially larger noise threshold compared to a standard search algorithm in a noisy environment. We use numerical simulations to characterize the level of noise tolerance via reinforcement in the presence of both coherent and incoherent noise, considering a system of $N$ qubits and a single $D$-level (qudit) system. Our results show that reinforcement significantly enhances the algorithm's success probability and improves the scaling of its computation time with system size. These findings indicate that reinforcement offers a promising strategy for error mitigation, especially when a precise noise model is unavailable.

### [208] [Measurement-enhanced entanglement in a monitored superconducting chain](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.04375)
*Rui-Jing Guo,Ji-Yao Chen,Zhi-Yuan Wei*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该研究表明，在受监控的量子动力学中，局部测量可能增强而非抑制纠缠增长。在一维自旋费米子链中，BCS配对与自旋分辨电荷测量之间的竞争导致测量增强的纠缠现象，但该效应在热力学极限下不持续。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统观点认为局部测量会抑制纠缠增长，但本研究旨在挑战这一直觉。通过分析一维自旋费米子链中BCS配对与连续测量的相互作用，探索测量可能增强纠缠的机制。

Method: 采用自由费米子模拟（free-fermion simulations）和准粒子分析（quasiparticle analysis）研究系统动力学。同时使用非线性sigma模型计算（nonlinear sigma-model calculation）分析稳态纠缠标度行为。

Result: 研究发现配对抑制纠缠增长，而测量抑制配对，两者的竞争导致测量增强的纠缠现象。对于Δ>0，稳态纠缠S_s在有限区间0<γ<γ_peak内随测量率γ增加而增加。在Δ>0且小但有限的γ下，稳态纠缠标度为S_s∼ln²L。

Conclusion: 测量增强的纠缠现象源于配对与测量之间的竞争机制，但该效应在热力学极限下不持续。这表明在特定参数条件下，局部测量可能意外地增强而非抑制纠缠增长。

Abstract: A common view in monitored quantum dynamics is that local measurements suppress entanglement growth. We show that this intuition can fail in a one-dimensional spinful fermionic chain governed by a BCS Hamiltonian with pairing strength $Δ$ and subject to continuous, on-site, spin-resolved charge measurements at rate $γ$. Using free-fermion simulations and quasiparticle analysis, we show that pairing suppresses entanglement growth, while measurements suppress pairing. Their competition yields measurement-enhanced entanglement: for $Δ>0$, the steady-state entanglement $S_s$ increases with $γ$ over a finite interval $0<γ<γ_{\rm peak}$. This occurs because stronger measurements suppress pairing correlations, which would otherwise suppress entanglement growth. Using a nonlinear sigma-model calculation and free-fermion simulations, we provide evidence that for $Δ>0$ and small but finite $γ$, the steady-state entanglement scales as $S_s\sim \ln^2 L$. This implies that, in this setting, measurement-enhanced entanglement does not persist in the thermodynamic limit.

</details>


### [209] [Digital-Analog Quantum Simulation and Computing: A Perspective on Past and Future Developments](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.04438)
*Lucas Lamata*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该论文综述了数字-模拟量子技术（digital-analog quantum technologies）这一新兴范式，该范式结合了数字量子计算的可扩展性和模拟量子计算的低误差优势，为近期和中期的量子模拟与计算提供了有前景的发展路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统量子模拟与计算主要基于数字（digital）和模拟（analog）两种范式，但各自存在局限性。数字范式虽然具有可扩展性和通用性，但误差累积快且需要纠错；模拟范式误差较低但演化选择有限且缺乏通用性。因此需要探索结合两者优势的新范式。

Method: 提出数字-模拟量子技术范式，将量子平台原生相互作用提供的大型模拟模块（large analog blocks）与数字门（digital gates）相结合。模拟模块利用平台固有相互作用实现多量子比特操作，数字门则提供灵活性和通用性。

Result: 该范式在过去十年中已发展成为量子模拟与计算领域的新兴研究方向。它通过结合两种传统范式的优势，为近期和中期的量子技术发展提供了有前景的可能性，既保持了模拟方法的低误差特性，又获得了数字方法的通用性。

Conclusion: 数字-模拟量子技术范式代表了量子计算领域的重要发展方向，它通过整合数字和模拟方法的优势，为构建更实用、可扩展的量子系统提供了新思路。论文展望了该领域未来的发展可能性。

Abstract: Quantum simulation and computing traditionally has been based on two main paradigms, namely, digital and analog. In the digital paradigm, usually single and two-qubit gates (where qubit is an acronym for quantum bit) are employed as building blocks for scalable, universal quantum computing, although errors add up fast and error correction will be ultimately needed for scaling up. In the analog paradigm, large analog blocks are normally employed for a unitary dynamics that carries out the computation, enabling quantum operations on many qubits with reduced errors, but with the drawback of a limited choice of evolutions and lack of universality. In the past decade, a new paradigm has emerged, showing interesting possibilities for quantum simulation and computing in the near and mid term. This is the paradigm of digital-analog quantum technologies, which proposes to combine the best of both paradigms: large analog blocks, provided by native interactions of the employed quantum platform, enabling scalability, combined with digital gates, allowing for more versatility and, ultimately, universality. In this Perspective, I give an overview of the evolution of the field along the past decade, and an outlook for its future possibilities.

</details>


### [210] [Quadrature-Symmetric PulsePol for Robust Quantum Control Beyond the Ideal Pulse Approximation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.04789)
*Mayur Jhamnani,Venkata SubbaRao Redrouthu,Jose P. Carvalho,Ethan Feldman,Anders B. Nielsen,Phani Kumar,Niels Chr. Nielsen,P. K. Madhu,Asif Equbal*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该研究重新分析了PulsePol量子控制方案在有限脉冲约束下的性能，发现其保真度显著下降。通过相位调整重建相互作用框架自旋哈密顿量的对称性，提出了Q-PulsePol方案，提高了对有限脉冲效应的鲁棒性和极化转移效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 先前对PulsePol脉冲序列的分析假设了理想化的瞬时微波脉冲，这在较高磁场下难以实现。需要重新评估有限脉冲约束下该方案的性能退化问题，并开发更实用的量子控制协议。

Method: 使用双模Floquet理论分析有限脉冲效应下的对称性破缺机制。通过相位调整重建相互作用框架自旋哈密顿量（interaction-frame spin Hamiltonian）的对称性，开发了Q-PulsePol序列，其中"Q"代表恢复的quadrature对称性。

Result: 研究显示PulsePol在有限脉冲约束下性能显著退化。Q-PulsePol方案展示了对有限脉冲效应的鲁棒性，并提高了极化转移效率，使其成为使用单模（零量子或双量子）转移实现固体中核自旋体超极化的实用可靠方案。

Conclusion: 该工作连接了理想化量子控制与现实的脉冲工程，为基于自旋的量子控制协议建立了设计规则。Q-PulsePol方案在有限脉冲条件下表现出优越性能，为固体核自旋超极化提供了更实用的解决方案。

Abstract: PulsePol is an elegantly designed pulse-sequence-based quantum control scheme that enables polarization transfer between electron and nuclear spins, for example, in nitrogen-vacancy (NV) centers. However, previous analyses of PulsePol assumed very strong, near-ideal, instantaneous microwave pulses, which is rarely achievable at higher magnetic fields. We revisit the PulsePol scheme under finite-pulse constraints and show that its performance significantly degrades due to finite-pulse effects. Using bimodal Floquet theory, we identify the symmetry-breaking mechanism responsible for this deterioration in fidelity. By phase adjustment, we reestablish the proper symmetry of the interaction-frame spin Hamiltonian, leading to a sequence called Q-PulsePol, where "Q" reflects the restored quadrature symmetry. Our results demonstrate robustness to finite-pulse effects and improved polarization transfer efficiency, establishing Q-PulsePol as a practical and reliable scheme for bulk hyperpolarization of nuclear spins in solids using a single-mode (zero-quantum or double-quantum) transfer. This work bridges idealized quantum control with realistic pulse engineering, establishing design rules for spin-based quantum control protocols.

### [211] [Modeling the non-Markovian Brownian motion of an optomechanical resonator](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.04856)
*Aritra Ghosh,Malay Bandyopadhyay,M. Bhattacharya*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种全局可接受的现象学浴谱密度（globally-admissible phenomenological spectral density），用于描述光机械谐振器的非马尔可夫布朗运动（non-Markovian Brownian motion）。该方法基于近共振实验观测的非欧姆谱（non-Ohmic spectrum），构建了一个在机械共振附近再现局部幂律行为（local-power-law behavior）且全局定义良好的模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机源于[Nat. Commun. 6, 7606 (2015)]中观测到的近共振非欧姆谱（near-resonance non-Ohmic spectrum）。需要避免朴素全局外推（naive global extrapolation）导致的发散问题，构建一个既能再现观测到的局部幂律行为，又在全局范围内定义良好的现象学浴谱密度。

Method: 构建了一个全局可接受的现象学浴谱密度（globally-admissible phenomenological spectral density），该密度在机械共振附近再现局部幂律行为（local-power-law behavior）。对应的结构化环境模型（structured environment model）产生了一个非局域机械响应函数（nonlocal mechanical susceptibility），其解析极点结构（analytic pole structure）编码了观测到的线宽（linewidth）。

Result: 所得耗散核（dissipation kernel）表现出幂律调制指数衰减（power-law-modulated exponential decay）并具有瞬态负性（transient negativity），表明存在强记忆效应（strong memory effects）。在弱耦合机制（weak-coupling regime）下，基于零差检测（homodyne detection）的光学读出（optical readout）可实现近共振光谱学（near-resonance spectroscopy），并通过校准驱动（calibrated drive）原则上可重建完整的机械响应函数。

Conclusion: 该研究提供了一条从局部推断谱特性（locally-inferred spectral properties）到全局可接受开放系统描述（globally-admissible open-system descriptions）的一致路径，并建立了一个在腔光力学（cavity optomechanics）中探测结构化环境（structured environments）的框架。

Abstract: We propose a globally-admissible phenomenological spectral density of the bath for the non-Markovian Brownian motion of an optomechanical resonator, motivated by the near-resonance experimental observation of a non-Ohmic spectrum in [Nat. Commun. 6, 7606 (2015)]. To avoid divergences arising from a naive global extrapolation, we construct this phenomenological bath spectral density that reproduces the observed local-power-law behavior near the mechanical resonance while remaining well defined globally, ensuring the finiteness of the bath-induced renormalizations and quadrature fluctuations of the resonator. The corresponding model of the structured environment produces a nonlocal mechanical susceptibility whose analytic pole structure encodes the observed linewidth. The resulting dissipation kernel exhibits a power-law-modulated exponential decay with transient negativity, signaling strong memory effects. In the weak-coupling regime, the optical readout based on homodyne detection enables near-resonance spectroscopy and, with a calibrated drive on the resonator, permits, in principle, the reconstruction of the full mechanical susceptibility, thereby providing access to both the dissipative and dispersive bath contributions. Our results provide a consistent route from locally-inferred spectral properties to globally-admissible open-system descriptions and establish a framework for probing structured environments in cavity optomechanics.

</details>
